<p class="normal">the context in which the personal data have been collected, in particular regarding the relationship between data subjects and the controller;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the nature of the personal data, in particular whether special categories of personal data are processed, pursuant to Article 9, or whether personal data related to criminal convictions and offences are processed, pursuant to Article 10;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(d)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the possible consequences of the intended further processing for data subjects;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(e)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the existence of appropriate safeguards, which may include encryption or pseudonymisation.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_7"></a>Article 7</h4>
<p class="ti-art"><strong>Conditions for consent</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where processing is based on consent, the controller shall be able to demonstrate that the data subject has consented to processing of his or her personal data.</p>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If the data subject’s consent is given in the context of a written declaration which also concerns other matters, the request for consent shall be presented in a manner which is clearly distinguishable from the other matters, in an intelligible and easily accessible form, using clear and plain language. Any part of such a declaration which constitutes an infringement of this Regulation shall not be binding.</p>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The data subject shall have the right to withdraw his or her consent at any time. The withdrawal of consent shall not affect the lawfulness of processing based on consent before its withdrawal. Prior to giving consent, the data subject shall be informed thereof. It shall be as easy to withdraw as to give consent.</p>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;When assessing whether consent is freely given, utmost account shall be taken of whether,&nbsp;<span class="italic">inter alia</span>, the performance of a contract, including the provision of a service, is conditional on consent to the processing of personal data that is not necessary for the performance of that contract.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_8"></a>Article 8</h4>
<p class="ti-art"><strong>Conditions applicable to child’s consent in relation to information society services</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where point (a) of Article 6(1) applies, in relation to the offer of information society services directly to a child, the processing of the personal data of a child shall be lawful where the child is at least 16 years old. Where the child is below the age of 16 years, such processing shall be lawful only if and to the extent that consent is given or authorised by the holder of parental responsibility over the child.</p>
<p class="normal">Member&nbsp;States may provide by law for a lower age for those purposes provided that such lower age is not below 13 years.</p>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The controller shall make reasonable efforts to verify in such cases that consent is given or authorised by the holder of parental responsibility over the child, taking into consideration available technology.</p>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Paragraph 1 shall not affect the general contract law of Member States such as the rules on the validity, formation or effect of a contract in relation to a child.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_9"></a>Article 9</h4>
<p class="ti-art"><strong>Processing of special categories of personal data</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Processing of personal data revealing racial or ethnic origin, political opinions, religious or philosophical beliefs, or trade union membership, and the processing of genetic data, biometric data for the purpose of uniquely identifying a natural person, data concerning health or data concerning a natural person’s sex life or sexual orientation shall be prohibited.</p>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Paragraph 1 shall not apply if one of the following applies:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the data subject has given explicit consent to the processing of those personal data for one or more specified purposes, except where Union or Member&nbsp;State law provide that the prohibition referred to in paragraph 1 may not be lifted by the data subject;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">processing is necessary for the purposes of carrying out the obligations and exercising specific rights of the controller or of the data subject in the field of employment and social security and social protection law in so far as it is authorised by Union or Member State law or a collective agreement pursuant to Member&nbsp;State law providing for appropriate safeguards for the fundamental rights and the interests of the data subject;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">processing is necessary to protect the vital interests of the data subject or of another natural person where the data subject is physically or legally incapable of giving consent;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(d)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">processing is carried out in the course of its legitimate activities with appropriate safeguards by a foundation, association or any other not-for-profit body with a political, philosophical, religious or trade union aim and on condition that the processing relates solely to the members or to former members of the body or to persons who have regular contact with it in connection with its purposes and that the personal data are not disclosed outside that body without the consent of the data subjects;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(e)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">processing relates to personal data which are manifestly made public by the data subject;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(f)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">processing is necessary for the establishment, exercise or defence of legal claims or whenever courts are acting in their judicial capacity;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(g)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">processing is necessary for reasons of substantial public interest, on the basis of Union or Member State law which shall be proportionate to the aim pursued, respect the essence of the right to data protection and provide for suitable and specific measures to safeguard the fundamental rights and the interests of the data subject;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(h)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">processing is necessary for the purposes of preventive or occupational medicine, for the assessment of the working capacity of the employee, medical diagnosis, the provision of health or social care or treatment or the management of health or social care systems and services on the basis of Union or Member&nbsp;State law or pursuant to contract with a health professional and subject to the conditions and safeguards referred to in paragraph&nbsp;3;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(i)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">processing is necessary for reasons of public interest in the area of public health, such as protecting against serious cross-border threats to health or ensuring high standards of quality and safety of health care and of medicinal products or medical devices, on the basis of Union or Member&nbsp;State law which provides for suitable and specific measures to safeguard the rights and freedoms of the data subject, in particular professional secrecy;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(j)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">processing is necessary for archiving purposes in the public interest, scientific or historical research purposes or statistical purposes in accordance with Article&nbsp;89(1) based on Union or Member State law which shall be proportionate to the aim pursued, respect the essence of the right to data protection and provide for suitable and specific measures to safeguard the fundamental rights and the interests of the data subject.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Personal data referred to in paragraph&nbsp;1 may be processed for the purposes referred to in point&nbsp;(h) of paragraph&nbsp;2 when those data are processed by or under the responsibility of a professional subject to the obligation of professional secrecy under Union or Member State law or rules established by national competent bodies or by another person also subject to an obligation of secrecy under Union or Member&nbsp;State law or rules established by national competent bodies.</p>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Member States may maintain or introduce further conditions, including limitations, with regard to the processing of genetic data, biometric data or data concerning health.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_10"></a>Article 10</h4>
<p class="ti-art"><strong>Processing of personal data relating to criminal convictions and offences</strong></p>
<p class="normal">Processing of personal data relating to criminal convictions and offences or related security measures based on Article&nbsp;6(1) shall be carried out only under the control of official authority or when the processing is authorised by Union or Member&nbsp;State law providing for appropriate safeguards for the rights and freedoms of data subjects. Any comprehensive register of criminal convictions shall be kept only under the control of official authority.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_11"></a>Article 11</h4>
<p class="ti-art"><strong>Processing which does not require identification</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If the purposes for which a controller processes personal data do not or do no longer require the identification of a data subject by the controller, the controller shall not be obliged to maintain, acquire or process additional information in order to identify the data subject for the sole purpose of complying with this Regulation.</p>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where, in cases referred to in paragraph 1 of this Article, the controller is able to demonstrate that it is not in a position to identify the data subject, the controller shall inform the data subject accordingly, if possible. In such cases, Articles 15 to 20 shall not apply except where the data subject, for the purpose of exercising his or her rights under those articles, provides additional information enabling his or her identification.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h2 id="d1e2161-1-1" class="ti-section-1"><span class="italic">CHAPTER III</span></h2>
<p class="ti-section-1"><strong><span class="bold"><span class="italic">Rights of the data subject</span></span></strong></p>
<h3 id="d1e2172-1-1" class="ti-section-1"><span class="expanded">Section 1</span></h3>
<p class="ti-section-1"><strong><span class="bold"><span class="expanded">Transparency and modalities</span></span></strong></p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_12"></a>Article 12</h4>
<p class="ti-art"><strong>Transparent information, communication and modalities for the exercise of the rights of the data subject</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The controller shall take appropriate measures to provide any information referred to in Articles&nbsp;13 and 14 and any communication under Articles 15 to 22 and 34 relating to processing to the data subject in a concise, transparent, intelligible and easily accessible form, using clear and plain language, in particular for any information addressed specifically to a child. The information shall be provided in writing, or by other means, including, where appropriate, by electronic means. When requested by the data subject, the information may be provided orally, provided that the identity of the data subject is proven by other means.</p>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The controller shall facilitate the exercise of data subject rights under Articles&nbsp;15 to 22. In the cases referred to in Article 11(2), the controller shall not refuse to act on the request of the data subject for exercising his or her rights under Articles 15 to 22, unless the controller demonstrates that it is not in a position to identify the data subject.</p>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The controller shall provide information on action taken on a request under Articles&nbsp;15 to&nbsp;22 to the data subject without undue delay and in any event within one month of receipt of the request. That period may be extended by two further months where necessary, taking into account the complexity and number of the requests. The controller shall inform the data subject of any such extension within one month of receipt of the request, together with the reasons for the delay. Where the data subject makes the request by electronic form means, the information shall be provided by electronic means where possible, unless otherwise requested by the data subject.</p>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If the controller does not take action on the request of the data subject, the controller shall inform the data subject without delay and at the latest within one month of receipt of the request of the reasons for not taking action and on the possibility of lodging a complaint with a supervisory authority and seeking a judicial remedy.</p>
<p class="normal">5.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Information provided under Articles 13 and 14 and any communication and any actions taken under Articles 15 to 22 and 34 shall be provided free of charge. Where requests from a data subject are manifestly unfounded or excessive, in particular because of their repetitive character, the controller may either:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">charge a reasonable fee taking into account the administrative costs of providing the information or communication or taking the action requested; or</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">refuse to act on the request.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">The controller shall bear the burden of demonstrating the manifestly unfounded or excessive character of the request.</p>
<p class="normal">6.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Without prejudice to Article 11, where the controller has reasonable doubts concerning the identity of the natural person making the request referred to in Articles 15 to 21, the controller may request the provision of additional information necessary to confirm the identity of the data subject.</p>
<p class="normal">7.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The information to be provided to data subjects pursuant to Articles 13 and 14 may be provided in combination with standardised icons in order to give in an easily visible, intelligible and clearly legible manner a meaningful overview of the intended processing. Where the icons are presented electronically they shall be machine-readable.</p>
<p class="normal">8.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Commission shall be empowered to adopt delegated acts in accordance with Article&nbsp;92 for the purpose of determining the information to be presented by the icons and the procedures for providing standardised icons.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h3 id="d1e2244-1-1" class="ti-section-1"><span class="expanded">Section 2</span></h3>
<p id="L_2016119EN.01000101-d-005" class="ti-section-2"><strong><span class="bold"><span class="expanded">Information and access to personal data</span></span></strong></p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_13"></a>Article 13</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Information to be provided where personal data are collected from the data subject</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where personal data relating to a data subject are collected from the data subject, the controller shall, at the time when personal data are obtained, provide the data subject with all of the following information:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the identity and the contact details of the controller and, where applicable, of the controller’s representative;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the contact details of the data protection officer, where applicable;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the purposes of the processing for which the personal data are intended as well as the legal basis for the processing;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(d)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">where the processing is based on point (f) of Article 6(1), the legitimate interests pursued by the controller or by a third party;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(e)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the recipients or categories of recipients of the personal data, if any;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(f)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">where applicable, the fact that the controller intends to transfer personal data to a third country or international organisation and the existence or absence of an adequacy decision by the Commission, or in the case of transfers referred to in Article&nbsp;46 or 47, or the second subparagraph of Article&nbsp;49(1), reference to the appropriate or suitable safeguards and the means by which to obtain a copy of them or where they have been made available.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In addition to the information referred to in paragraph 1, the controller shall, at the time when personal data are obtained, provide the data subject with the following further information necessary to ensure fair and transparent processing:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the period for which the personal data will be stored, or if that is not possible, the criteria used to determine that period;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the existence of the right to request from the controller access to and rectification or erasure of personal data or restriction of processing concerning the data subject or to object to processing as well as the right to data portability;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">where the processing is based on point (a) of Article 6(1) or point (a) of Article&nbsp;9(2), the existence of the right to withdraw consent at any time, without affecting the lawfulness of processing based on consent before its withdrawal;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(d)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the right to lodge a complaint with a supervisory authority;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(e)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">whether the provision of personal data is a statutory or contractual requirement, or a requirement necessary to enter into a contract, as well as whether the data subject is obliged to provide the personal data and of the possible consequences of failure to provide such data;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(f)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the existence of automated decision-making, including profiling, referred to in Article 22(1) and (4) and, at least in those cases, meaningful information about the logic involved, as well as the significance and the envisaged consequences of such processing for the data subject.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where the controller intends to further process the personal data for a purpose other than that for which the personal data were collected, the controller shall provide the data subject prior to that further processing with information on that other purpose and with any relevant further information as referred to in paragraph 2.</p>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Paragraphs 1, 2 and 3 shall not apply where and insofar as the data subject already has the information.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_14"></a>Article 14</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Information to be provided where personal data have not been obtained from the data subject</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where personal data have not been obtained from the data subject, the controller shall provide the data subject with the following information:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the identity and the contact details of the controller and, where applicable, of the controller’s representative;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the contact details of the data protection officer, where applicable;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the purposes of the processing for which the personal data are intended as well as the legal basis for the processing;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(d)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the categories of personal data concerned;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(e)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the recipients or categories of recipients of the personal data, if any;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(f)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">where applicable, that the controller intends to transfer personal data to a recipient in a third country or international organisation and the existence or absence of an adequacy decision by the Commission, or in the case of transfers referred to in Article&nbsp;46 or 47, or the second subparagraph of Article 49(1), reference to the appropriate or suitable safeguards and the means to obtain a copy of them or where they have been made available.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In addition to the information referred to in paragraph 1, the controller shall provide the data subject with the following information necessary to ensure fair and transparent processing in respect of the data subject:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the period for which the personal data will be stored, or if that is not possible, the criteria used to determine that period;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">where the processing is based on point (f) of Article 6(1), the legitimate interests pursued by the controller or by a third party;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the existence of the right to request from the controller access to and rectification or erasure of personal data or restriction of processing concerning the data subject and to object to processing as well as the right to data portability;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(d)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">where processing is based on point (a) of Article 6(1) or point (a) of Article 9(2), the existence of the right to withdraw consent at any time, without affecting the lawfulness of processing based on consent before its withdrawal;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(e)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the right to lodge a complaint with a supervisory authority;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(f)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">from which source the personal data originate, and if applicable, whether it came from publicly accessible sources;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(g)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the existence of automated decision-making, including profiling, referred to in Article&nbsp;22(1) and (4) and, at least in those cases, meaningful information about the logic involved, as well as the significance and the envisaged consequences of such processing for the data subject.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The controller shall provide the information referred to in paragraphs 1 and 2:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">within a reasonable period after obtaining the personal data, but at the latest within one month, having regard to the specific circumstances in which the personal data are processed;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">if the personal data are to be used for communication with the data subject, at the latest at the time of the first communication to that data subject; or</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">if a disclosure to another recipient is envisaged, at the latest when the personal data are first disclosed.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where the controller intends to further process the personal data for a purpose other than that for which the personal data were obtained, the controller shall provide the data subject prior to that further processing with information on that other purpose and with any relevant further information as referred to in paragraph&nbsp;2.</p>
<p class="normal">5.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Paragraphs 1 to 4 shall not apply where and insofar as:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the data subject already has the information;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the provision of such information proves impossible or would involve a disproportionate effort, in particular for processing for archiving purposes in the public interest, scientific or historical research purposes or statistical purposes, subject to the conditions and safeguards referred to in Article 89(1) or in so far as the obligation referred to in paragraph&nbsp;1 of this Article is likely to render impossible or seriously impair the achievement of the objectives of that processing. In such cases the controller shall take appropriate measures to protect the data subject’s rights and freedoms and legitimate interests, including making the information publicly available;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">obtaining or disclosure is expressly laid down by Union or Member&nbsp;State law to which the controller is subject and which provides appropriate measures to protect the data subject’s legitimate interests; or</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(d)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">where the personal data must remain confidential subject to an obligation of professional secrecy regulated by Union or Member&nbsp;State law, including a statutory obligation of secrecy.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_15"></a>Article 15</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Right of access by the data subject</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The data subject shall have the right to obtain from the controller confirmation as to whether or not personal data concerning him or her are being processed, and, where that is the case, access to the personal data and the following information:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the purposes of the processing;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the categories of personal data concerned;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the recipients or categories of recipient to whom the personal data have been or will be disclosed, in particular recipients in third countries or international organisations;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(d)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">where possible, the envisaged period for which the personal data will be stored, or, if not possible, the criteria used to determine that period;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(e)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the existence of the right to request from the controller rectification or erasure of personal data or restriction of processing of personal data concerning the data subject or to object to such processing;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(f)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the right to lodge a complaint with a supervisory authority;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(g)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">where the personal data are not collected from the data subject, any available information as to their source;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(h)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the existence of automated decision-making, including profiling, referred to in Article&nbsp;22(1) and (4) and, at least in those cases, meaningful information about the logic involved, as well as the significance and the envisaged consequences of such processing for the data subject.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where personal data are transferred to a third country or to an international organisation, the data subject shall have the right to be informed of the appropriate safeguards pursuant to Article 46 relating to the transfer.</p>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The controller shall provide a copy of the personal data undergoing processing. For any further copies requested by the data subject, the controller may charge a reasonable fee based on administrative costs. Where the data subject makes the request by electronic means, and unless otherwise requested by the data subject, the information shall be provided in a commonly used electronic form.</p>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The right to obtain a copy referred to in paragraph 3 shall not adversely affect the rights and freedoms of others.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h3 id="d1e2589-1-1" class="ti-section-1"><span class="expanded">Section 3</span></h3>
<p id="L_2016119EN.01000101-d-006" class="ti-section-2"><strong><span class="bold"><span class="expanded">Rectification and erasure</span></span></strong></p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_16"></a>Article 16</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Right to rectification</strong></p>
<p class="normal">The data subject shall have the right to obtain from the controller without undue delay the rectification of inaccurate personal data concerning him or her. Taking into account the purposes of the processing, the data subject shall have the right to have incomplete personal data completed, including by means of providing a supplementary statement.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_17"></a>Article 17</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Right to erasure (‘right to be forgotten’)</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The data subject shall have the right to obtain from the controller the erasure of personal data concerning him or her without undue delay and the controller shall have the obligation to erase personal data without undue delay where one of the following grounds applies:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the personal data are no longer necessary in relation to the purposes for which they were collected or otherwise processed;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the data subject withdraws consent on which the processing is based according to point&nbsp;(a) of Article 6(1), or point&nbsp;(a) of Article 9(2), and where there is no other legal ground for the processing;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the data subject objects to the processing pursuant to Article 21(1) and there are no overriding legitimate grounds for the processing, or the data subject objects to the processing pursuant to Article 21(2);</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(d)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the personal data have been unlawfully processed;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(e)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the personal data have to be erased for compliance with a legal obligation in Union or Member&nbsp;State law to which the controller is subject;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(f)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the personal data have been collected in relation to the offer of information society services referred to in Article&nbsp;8(1).</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where the controller has made the personal data public and is obliged pursuant to paragraph&nbsp;1 to erase the personal data, the controller, taking account of available technology and the cost of implementation, shall take reasonable steps, including technical measures, to inform controllers which are processing the personal data that the data subject has requested the erasure by such controllers of any links to, or copy or replication of, those personal data.</p>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Paragraphs 1 and 2 shall not apply to the extent that processing is necessary:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">for exercising the right of freedom of expression and information;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">for compliance with a legal obligation which requires processing by Union or Member&nbsp;State law to which the controller is subject or for the performance of a task carried out in the public interest or in the exercise of official authority vested in the controller;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">for reasons of public interest in the area of public health in accordance with points&nbsp;(h) and (i) of Article 9(2) as well as Article 9(3);</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(d)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">for archiving purposes in the public interest, scientific or historical research purposes or statistical purposes in accordance with Article 89(1) in so far as the right referred to in paragraph&nbsp;1 is likely to render impossible or seriously impair the achievement of the objectives of that processing; or</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(e)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">for the establishment, exercise or defence of legal claims.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_18"></a>Article 18</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Right to restriction of processing</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The data subject shall have the right to obtain from the controller restriction of processing where one of the following applies:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the accuracy of the personal data is contested by the data subject, for a period enabling the controller to verify the accuracy of the personal data;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the processing is unlawful and the data subject opposes the erasure of the personal data and requests the restriction of their use instead;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the controller no longer needs the personal data for the purposes of the processing, but they are required by the data subject for the establishment, exercise or defence of legal claims;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(d)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the data subject has objected to processing pursuant to Article&nbsp;21(1) pending the verification whether the legitimate grounds of the controller override those of the data subject.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where processing has been restricted under paragraph 1, such personal data shall, with the exception of storage, only be processed with the data subject’s consent or for the establishment, exercise or defence of legal claims or for the protection of the rights of another natural or legal person or for reasons of important public interest of the Union or of a Member&nbsp;State.</p>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;A data subject who has obtained restriction of processing pursuant to paragraph&nbsp;1 shall be informed by the controller before the restriction of processing is lifted.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_19"></a>Article 19</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Notification obligation regarding rectification or erasure of personal data or restriction of processing</strong></p>
<p class="normal">The controller shall communicate any rectification or erasure of personal data or restriction of processing carried out in accordance with Article&nbsp;16, Article 17(1) and Article 18 to each recipient to whom the personal data have been disclosed, unless this proves impossible or involves disproportionate effort. The controller shall inform the data subject about those recipients if the data subject requests it.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_20"></a>Article 20</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Right to data portability</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The data subject shall have the right to receive the personal data concerning him or her, which he or she has provided to a controller, in a structured, commonly used and machine-readable format and have the right to transmit those data to another controller without hindrance from the controller to which the personal data have been provided, where:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the processing is based on consent pursuant to point (a) of Article 6(1) or point&nbsp;(a) of Article 9(2) or on a contract pursuant to point (b) of Article 6(1); and</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the processing is carried out by automated means.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In exercising his or her right to data portability pursuant to paragraph 1, the data subject shall have the right to have the personal data transmitted directly from one controller to another, where technically feasible.</p>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The exercise of the right referred to in paragraph&nbsp;1 of this Article shall be without prejudice to Article&nbsp;17. That right shall not apply to processing necessary for the performance of a task carried out in the public interest or in the exercise of official authority vested in the controller.</p>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The right referred to in paragraph&nbsp;1 shall not adversely affect the rights and freedoms of others.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h3 id="d1e2793-1-1" class="ti-section-1"><span class="expanded">Section 4</span></h3>
<p id="L_2016119EN.01000101-d-007" class="ti-section-2"><strong><span class="bold"><span class="expanded">Right to object and automated individual decision-making</span></span></strong></p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_21"></a>Article 21</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Right to object</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The data subject shall have the right to object, on grounds relating to his or her particular situation, at any time to processing of personal data concerning him or her which is based on point (e) or (f) of Article 6(1), including profiling based on those provisions. The controller shall no longer process the personal data unless the controller demonstrates compelling legitimate grounds for the processing which override the interests, rights and freedoms of the data subject or for the establishment, exercise or defence of legal claims.</p>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where personal data are processed for direct marketing purposes, the data subject shall have the right to object at any time to processing of personal data concerning him or her for such marketing, which includes profiling to the extent that it is related to such direct marketing.</p>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where the data subject objects to processing for direct marketing purposes, the personal data shall no longer be processed for such purposes.</p>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;At the latest at the time of the first communication with the data subject, the right referred to in paragraphs&nbsp;1 and 2 shall be explicitly brought to the attention of the data subject and shall be presented clearly and separately from any other information.</p>
<p class="normal">5.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In the context of the use of information society services, and notwithstanding Directive&nbsp;2002/58/EC, the data subject may exercise his or her right to object by automated means using technical specifications.</p>
<p class="normal">6.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where personal data are processed for scientific or historical research purposes or statistical purposes pursuant to Article&nbsp;89(1), the data subject, on grounds relating to his or her particular situation, shall have the right to object to processing of personal data concerning him or her, unless the processing is necessary for the performance of a task carried out for reasons of public interest.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_22"></a>Article 22</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Automated individual decision-making, including profiling</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The data subject shall have the right not to be subject to a decision based solely on automated processing, including profiling, which produces legal effects concerning him or her or similarly significantly affects him or her.</p>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Paragraph&nbsp;1 shall not apply if the decision:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">is necessary for entering into, or performance of, a contract between the data subject and a data controller;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">is authorised by Union or Member&nbsp;State law to which the controller is subject and which also lays down suitable measures to safeguard the data subject’s rights and freedoms and legitimate interests; or</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<h3 class="normal">is based on the data subject’s explicit consent.</h3>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In the cases referred to in points (a) and (c) of paragraph&nbsp;2, the data controller shall implement suitable measures to safeguard the data subject’s rights and freedoms and legitimate interests, at least the right to obtain human intervention on the part of the controller, to express his or her point of view and to contest the decision.</p>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Decisions referred to in paragraph 2 shall not be based on special categories of personal data referred to in Article&nbsp;9(1), unless point (a) or (g) of Article 9(2) applies and suitable measures to safeguard the data subject’s rights and freedoms and legitimate interests are in place.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h3 id="d1e2884-1-1" class="ti-section-1"><span class="expanded">Section 5</span></h3>
<p id="L_2016119EN.01000101-d-008" class="ti-section-2"><strong><span class="bold"><span class="expanded">Restrictions</span></span></strong></p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_23"></a>Article 23</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Restrictions</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Union or Member&nbsp;State law to which the data controller or processor is subject may restrict by way of a legislative measure the scope of the obligations and rights provided for in Articles&nbsp;12 to 22 and Article&nbsp;34, as well as Article&nbsp;5 in so far as its provisions correspond to the rights and obligations provided for in Articles&nbsp;12 to 22, when such a restriction respects the essence of the fundamental rights and freedoms and is a necessary and proportionate measure in a democratic society to safeguard:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">national security;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">defence;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">public security;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(d)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the prevention, investigation, detection or prosecution of criminal offences or the execution of criminal penalties, including the safeguarding against and the prevention of threats to public security;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(e)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">other important objectives of general public interest of the Union or of a Member&nbsp;State, in particular an important economic or financial interest of the Union or of a Member&nbsp;State, including monetary, budgetary and taxation a matters, public health and social security;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(f)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the protection of judicial independence and judicial proceedings;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(g)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the prevention, investigation, detection and prosecution of breaches of ethics for regulated professions;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(h)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">a monitoring, inspection or regulatory function connected, even occasionally, to the exercise of official authority in the cases referred to in points (a) to (e) and&nbsp;(g);</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(i)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the protection of the data subject or the rights and freedoms of others;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(j)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the enforcement of civil law claims.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In particular, any legislative measure referred to in paragraph 1 shall contain specific provisions at least, where relevant, as to:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the purposes of the processing or categories of processing;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the categories of personal data;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the scope of the restrictions introduced;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(d)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the safeguards to prevent abuse or unlawful access or transfer;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(e)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the specification of the controller or categories of controllers;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(f)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the storage periods and the applicable safeguards taking into account the nature, scope and purposes of the processing or categories of processing;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(g)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the risks to the rights and freedoms of data subjects; and</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(h)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the right of data subjects to be informed about the restriction, unless that may be prejudicial to the purpose of the restriction.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h2 id="d1e3022-1-1" class="ti-section-1"><span class="italic">CHAPTER IV</span></h2>
<p id="L_2016119EN.01000101-d-009" class="ti-section-2"><strong><span class="bold"><span class="italic">Controller and processor</span></span></strong></p>
<h3 id="d1e3033-1-1" class="ti-section-1"><span class="expanded">Section 1</span></h3>
<p id="L_2016119EN.01000101-d-010" class="ti-section-2"><strong><span class="bold"><span class="expanded">General obligations</span></span></strong></p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_24"></a>Article 24</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Responsibility of the controller</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Taking into account the nature, scope, context and purposes of processing as well as the risks of varying likelihood and severity for the rights and freedoms of natural persons, the controller shall implement appropriate technical and organisational measures to ensure and to be able to demonstrate that processing is performed in accordance with this Regulation. Those measures shall be reviewed and updated where necessary.</p>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where proportionate in relation to processing activities, the measures referred to in paragraph&nbsp;1 shall include the implementation of appropriate data protection policies by the controller.</p>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Adherence to approved codes of conduct as referred to in Article&nbsp;40 or approved certification mechanisms as referred to in Article&nbsp;42 may be used as an element by which to demonstrate compliance with the obligations of the controller.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_25"></a>Article 25</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Data protection by design and by default</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Taking into account the state of the art, the cost of implementation and the nature, scope, context and purposes of processing as well as the risks of varying likelihood and severity for rights and freedoms of natural persons posed by the processing, the controller shall, both at the time of the determination of the means for processing and at the time of the processing itself, implement appropriate technical and organisational measures, such as pseudonymisation, which are designed to implement data-protection principles, such as data minimisation, in an effective manner and to integrate the necessary safeguards into the processing in order to meet the requirements of this Regulation and protect the rights of data subjects.</p>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The controller shall implement appropriate technical and organisational measures for ensuring that, by default, only personal data which are necessary for each specific purpose of the processing are processed. That obligation applies to the amount of personal data collected, the extent of their processing, the period of their storage and their accessibility. In particular, such measures shall ensure that by default personal data are not made accessible without the individual’s intervention to an indefinite number of natural persons.</p>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;An approved certification mechanism pursuant to Article&nbsp;42 may be used as an element to demonstrate compliance with the requirements set out in paragraphs&nbsp;1 and 2 of this Article.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_26"></a>Article 26</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Joint controllers</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where two or more controllers jointly determine the purposes and means of processing, they shall be joint controllers. They shall in a transparent manner determine their respective responsibilities for compliance with the obligations under this Regulation, in particular as regards the exercising of the rights of the data subject and their respective duties to provide the information referred to in Articles&nbsp;13 and 14, by means of an arrangement between them unless, and in so far as, the respective responsibilities of the controllers are determined by Union or Member&nbsp;State law to which the controllers are subject. The arrangement may designate a contact point for data subjects.</p>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The arrangement referred to in paragraph 1 shall duly reflect the respective roles and relationships of the joint controllers&nbsp;<span class="italic">vis-à-vis</span>&nbsp;the data subjects. The essence of the arrangement shall be made available to the data subject.</p>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Irrespective of the terms of the arrangement referred to in paragraph 1, the data subject may exercise his or her rights under this Regulation in respect of and against each of the controllers.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_27"></a>Article 27</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Representatives of controllers or processors not established in the Union</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where Article 3(2) applies, the controller or the processor shall designate in writing a representative in the Union.</p>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The obligation laid down in paragraph 1 of this Article shall not apply to:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">processing which is occasional, does not include, on a large scale, processing of special categories of data as referred to in Article 9(1) or processing of personal data relating to criminal convictions and offences referred to in Article 10, and is unlikely to result in a risk to the rights and freedoms of natural persons, taking into account the nature, context, scope and purposes of the processing; or</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">a public authority or body.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The representative shall be established in one of the Member States where the data subjects, whose personal data are processed in relation to the offering of goods or services to them, or whose behaviour is monitored, are.</p>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The representative shall be mandated by the controller or processor to be addressed in addition to or instead of the controller or the processor by, in particular, supervisory authorities and data subjects, on all issues related to processing, for the purposes of ensuring compliance with this Regulation.</p>
<p class="normal">5.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The designation of a representative by the controller or processor shall be without prejudice to legal actions which could be initiated against the controller or the processor themselves.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_28"></a>Article 28</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Processor</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where processing is to be carried out on behalf of a controller, the controller shall use only processors providing sufficient guarantees to implement appropriate technical and organisational measures in such a manner that processing will meet the requirements of this Regulation and ensure the protection of the rights of the data subject.</p>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The processor shall not engage another processor without prior specific or general written authorisation of the controller. In the case of general written authorisation, the processor shall inform the controller of any intended changes concerning the addition or replacement of other processors, thereby giving the controller the opportunity to object to such changes.</p>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Processing by a processor shall be governed by a contract or other legal act under Union or Member&nbsp;State law, that is binding on the processor with regard to the controller and that sets out the subject-matter and duration of the processing, the nature and purpose of the processing, the type of personal data and categories of data subjects and the obligations and rights of the controller. That contract or other legal act shall stipulate, in particular, that the processor:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">processes the personal data only on documented instructions from the controller, including with regard to transfers of personal data to a third country or an international organisation, unless required to do so by Union or Member&nbsp;State law to which the processor is subject; in such a case, the processor shall inform the controller of that legal requirement before processing, unless that law prohibits such information on important grounds of public interest;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">ensures that persons authorised to process the personal data have committed themselves to confidentiality or are under an appropriate statutory obligation of confidentiality;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">takes all measures required pursuant to Article 32;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(d)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">respects the conditions referred to in paragraphs 2 and 4 for engaging another processor;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(e)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">taking into account the nature of the processing, assists the controller by appropriate technical and organisational measures, insofar as this is possible, for the fulfilment of the controller’s obligation to respond to requests for exercising the data subject’s rights laid down in Chapter III;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(f)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">assists the controller in ensuring compliance with the obligations pursuant to Articles&nbsp;32 to 36 taking into account the nature of processing and the information available to the processor;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(g)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">at the choice of the controller, deletes or returns all the personal data to the controller after the end of the provision of services relating to processing, and deletes existing copies unless Union or Member State law requires storage of the personal data;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(h)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">makes available to the controller all information necessary to demonstrate compliance with the obligations laid down in this Article and allow for and contribute to audits, including inspections, conducted by the controller or another auditor mandated by the controller.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">With regard to point&nbsp;(h) of the first subparagraph, the processor shall immediately inform the controller if, in its opinion, an instruction infringes this Regulation or other Union or Member&nbsp;State data protection provisions.</p>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where a processor engages another processor for carrying out specific processing activities on behalf of the controller, the same data protection obligations as set out in the contract or other legal act between the controller and the processor as referred to in paragraph 3 shall be imposed on that other processor by way of a contract or other legal act under Union or Member State law, in particular providing sufficient guarantees to implement appropriate technical and organisational measures in such a manner that the processing will meet the requirements of this Regulation. Where that other processor fails to fulfil its data protection obligations, the initial processor shall remain fully liable to the controller for the performance of that other processor’s obligations.</p>
<p class="normal">5.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Adherence of a processor to an approved code of conduct as referred to in Article&nbsp;40 or an approved certification mechanism as referred to in Article&nbsp;42 may be used as an element by which to demonstrate sufficient guarantees as referred to in paragraphs&nbsp;1 and&nbsp;4 of this&nbsp;Article.</p>
<p class="normal">6.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Without prejudice to an individual contract between the controller and the processor, the contract or the other legal act referred to in paragraphs 3 and 4 of this Article may be based, in whole or in part, on standard contractual clauses referred to in paragraphs&nbsp;7 and&nbsp;8 of this Article, including when they are part of a certification granted to the controller or processor pursuant to Articles 42 and 43.</p>
<p class="normal">7.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Commission may lay down standard contractual clauses for the matters referred to in paragraph 3 and 4 of this Article and in accordance with the examination procedure referred to in Article 93(2).</p>
<p class="normal">8.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;A supervisory authority may adopt standard contractual clauses for the matters referred to in paragraph 3 and 4 of this Article and in accordance with the consistency mechanism referred to in Article&nbsp;63.</p>
<p class="normal">9.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The contract or the other legal act referred to in paragraphs 3 and 4 shall be in writing, including in electronic form.</p>
<p class="normal">10.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Without prejudice to Articles 82, 83 and 84, if a processor infringes this Regulation by determining the purposes and means of processing, the processor shall be considered to be a controller in respect of that processing.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_29"></a>Article 29</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Processing under the authority of the controller or processor</strong></p>
<p class="normal">The processor and any person acting under the authority of the controller or of the processor, who has access to personal data, shall not process those data except on instructions from the controller, unless required to do so by Union or Member&nbsp;State law.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_30"></a>Article 30</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Records of processing activities</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Each controller and, where applicable, the controller’s representative, shall maintain a record of processing activities under its responsibility. That record shall contain all of the following information:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the name and contact details of the controller and, where applicable, the joint controller, the controller’s representative and the data protection officer;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the purposes of the processing;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
