<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">a description of the categories of data subjects and of the categories of personal data;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(d)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the categories of recipients to whom the personal data have been or will be disclosed including recipients in third countries or international organisations;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(e)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">where applicable, transfers of personal data to a third country or an international organisation, including the identification of that third country or international organisation and, in the case of transfers referred to in the second subparagraph of Article&nbsp;49(1), the documentation of suitable safeguards;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(f)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">where possible, the envisaged time limits for erasure of the different categories of data;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(g)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">where possible, a general description of the technical and organisational security measures referred to in Article&nbsp;32(1).</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Each processor and, where applicable, the processor’s representative shall maintain a record of all categories of processing activities carried out on behalf of a controller, containing:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the name and contact details of the processor or processors and of each controller on behalf of which the processor is acting, and, where applicable, of the controller’s or the processor’s representative, and the data protection officer;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the categories of processing carried out on behalf of each controller;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">where applicable, transfers of personal data to a third country or an international organisation, including the identification of that third country or international organisation and, in the case of transfers referred to in the second subparagraph of Article&nbsp;49(1), the documentation of suitable safeguards;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(d)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">where possible, a general description of the technical and organisational security measures referred to in Article&nbsp;32(1).</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The records referred to in paragraphs 1 and 2 shall be in writing, including in electronic form.</p>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The controller or the processor and, where applicable, the controller’s or the processor’s representative, shall make the record available to the supervisory authority on request.</p>
<p class="normal">5.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The obligations referred to in paragraphs 1 and 2 shall not apply to an enterprise or an organisation employing fewer than 250 persons unless the processing it carries out is likely to result in a risk to the rights and freedoms of data&nbsp;subjects, the processing is not occasional, or the processing includes special categories of data as referred to in Article&nbsp;9(1) or personal data relating to criminal convictions and offences referred to in Article&nbsp;10.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_31"></a>Article 31</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Cooperation with the supervisory authority</strong></p>
<p class="normal">The controller and the processor and, where applicable, their representatives, shall cooperate, on request, with the supervisory authority in the performance of its tasks.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h3 id="d1e3373-1-1" class="ti-section-1"><span class="expanded">Section 2</span></h3>
<p id="L_2016119EN.01000101-d-011" class="ti-section-2"><strong><span class="bold"><span class="expanded">Security of personal data</span></span></strong></p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_32"></a>Article 32</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Security of processing</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Taking into account the state of the art, the costs of implementation and the nature, scope, context and purposes of processing as well as the risk of varying likelihood and severity for the rights and freedoms of natural persons, the controller and the processor shall implement appropriate technical and organisational measures to ensure a level of security appropriate to the risk, including inter alia as appropriate:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the pseudonymisation and encryption of personal data;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the ability to ensure the ongoing confidentiality, integrity, availability and resilience of processing systems and services;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the ability to restore the availability and access to personal data in a timely manner in the event of a physical or technical incident;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(d)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">a process for regularly testing, assessing and evaluating the effectiveness of technical and organisational measures for ensuring the security of the processing.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In assessing the appropriate level of security account shall be taken in particular of the risks that are presented by processing, in particular from accidental or unlawful destruction, loss, alteration, unauthorised disclosure of, or access to personal data transmitted, stored or otherwise processed.</p>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Adherence to an approved code of conduct as referred to in Article 40 or an approved certification mechanism as referred to in Article 42 may be used as an element by which to demonstrate compliance with the requirements set out in paragraph 1 of this Article.</p>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The controller and processor shall take steps to ensure that any natural person acting under the authority of the controller or the processor who has access to personal data does not process them except on instructions from the controller, unless he or she is required to do so by Union or Member State law.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_33"></a>Article 33</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Notification of a personal data breach to the supervisory authority</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In the case of a personal data breach, the controller shall without undue delay and, where feasible, not later than 72 hours after having become aware of it, notify the personal data breach to the supervisory authority competent in accordance with Article&nbsp;55, unless the personal data breach is unlikely to result in a risk to the rights and freedoms of natural persons. Where the notification to the supervisory authority is not made within 72&nbsp;hours, it shall be accompanied by reasons for the delay.</p>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The processor shall notify the controller without undue delay after becoming aware of a personal data breach.</p>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The notification referred to in paragraph 1 shall at least:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">describe the nature of the personal data breach including where possible, the categories and approximate number of data subjects concerned and the categories and approximate number of personal data records concerned;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">communicate the name and contact details of the data protection officer or other contact point where more information can be obtained;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">describe the likely consequences of the personal data breach;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(d)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">describe the measures taken or proposed to be taken by the controller to address the personal data breach, including, where appropriate, measures to mitigate its possible adverse effects.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where, and in so far as, it is not possible to provide the information at the same time, the information may be provided in phases without undue further delay.</p>
<p class="normal">5.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The controller shall document any personal data breaches, comprising the facts relating to the personal data breach, its effects and the remedial action taken. That documentation shall enable the supervisory authority to verify compliance with this Article.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_34"></a>Article 34</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Communication of a personal data breach to the data subject</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;When the personal data breach is likely to result in a high risk to the rights and freedoms of natural persons, the controller shall communicate the personal data breach to the data subject without undue delay.</p>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The communication to the data subject referred to in paragraph 1 of this Article shall describe in clear and plain language the nature of the personal data breach and contain at least the information and measures referred to in points&nbsp;(b), (c) and (d) of Article&nbsp;33(3).</p>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The communication to the data subject referred to in paragraph&nbsp;1 shall not be required if any of the following conditions are met:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the controller has implemented appropriate technical and organisational protection measures, and those measures were applied to the personal data affected by the personal data breach, in particular those that render the personal data unintelligible to any person who is not authorised to access it, such as encryption;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the controller has taken subsequent measures which ensure that the high risk to the rights and freedoms of data subjects referred to in paragraph&nbsp;1 is no longer likely to materialise;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">it would involve disproportionate effort. In such a case, there shall instead be a public communication or similar measure whereby the data subjects are informed in an equally effective manner.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;If the controller has not already communicated the personal data breach to the data subject, the supervisory authority, having considered the likelihood of the personal data breach resulting in a high risk, may require it to do so or may decide that any of the conditions referred to in paragraph 3 are met.</p>
<p id="d1e3536-1-1" class="ti-section-1"><span class="expanded">Section 3</span></p>
<p id="L_2016119EN.01000101-d-012" class="ti-section-2"><span class="bold"><span class="expanded">Data protection impact assessment and prior consultation</span></span></p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_35"></a>Article 35</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Data protection impact assessment</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where a type of processing in particular using new technologies, and taking into account the nature, scope, context and purposes of the processing, is likely to result in a high risk to the rights and freedoms of natural persons, the controller shall, prior to the processing, carry out an assessment of the impact of the envisaged processing operations on the protection of personal data. A single assessment may address a set of similar processing operations that present similar high risks.</p>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The controller shall seek the advice of the data protection officer, where designated, when carrying out a data protection impact assessment.</p>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;A data protection impact assessment referred to in paragraph&nbsp;1 shall in particular be required in the case of:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">a systematic and extensive evaluation of personal aspects relating to natural persons which is based on automated processing, including profiling, and on which decisions are based that produce legal effects concerning the natural person or similarly significantly affect the natural person;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">processing on a large scale of special categories of data referred to in Article&nbsp;9(1), or of personal data relating to criminal convictions and offences referred to in Article&nbsp;10; or</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">a systematic monitoring of a publicly accessible area on a large scale.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The supervisory authority shall establish and make public a list of the kind of processing operations which are subject to the requirement for a data protection impact assessment pursuant to paragraph&nbsp;1. The supervisory authority shall communicate those lists to the&nbsp;Board referred to in Article 68.</p>
<p class="normal">5.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The supervisory authority may also establish and make public a list of the kind of processing operations for which no data protection impact assessment is required. The supervisory authority shall communicate those lists to the Board.</p>
<p class="normal">6.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Prior to the adoption of the lists referred to in paragraphs 4 and 5, the competent supervisory authority shall apply the consistency mechanism referred to in Article&nbsp;63 where such lists involve processing activities which are related to the offering of goods or services to data subjects or to the monitoring of their behaviour in several Member&nbsp;States, or may substantially affect the free movement of personal data within the Union.</p>
<p class="normal">7.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The assessment shall contain at least:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">a systematic description of the envisaged processing operations and the purposes of the processing, including, where applicable, the legitimate interest pursued by the controller;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">an assessment of the necessity and proportionality of the processing operations in relation to the purposes;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">an assessment of the risks to the rights and freedoms of data subjects referred to in paragraph&nbsp;1; and</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(d)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the measures envisaged to address the risks, including safeguards, security measures and mechanisms to ensure the protection of personal data and to demonstrate compliance with this Regulation taking into account the rights and legitimate interests of data subjects and other persons concerned.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">8.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Compliance with approved codes of conduct referred to in Article&nbsp;40 by the relevant controllers or processors shall be taken into due account in assessing the impact of the processing operations performed by such controllers or processors, in particular for the purposes of a data protection impact assessment.</p>
<p class="normal">9.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where appropriate, the controller shall seek the views of data subjects or their representatives on the intended processing, without prejudice to the protection of commercial or public interests or the security of processing operations.</p>
<p class="normal">10.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where processing pursuant to point (c) or (e) of Article 6(1) has a legal basis in Union law or in the law of the Member&nbsp;State to which the controller is subject, that law regulates the specific processing operation or set of operations in question, and a data protection impact assessment has already been carried out as part of a general impact assessment in the context of the adoption of that legal basis, paragraphs&nbsp;1 to 7 shall not apply unless Member&nbsp;States deem it to be necessary to carry out such an assessment prior to processing activities.</p>
<p class="normal">11.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where necessary, the controller shall carry out a review to assess if processing is performed in accordance with the data protection impact assessment at least when there is a change of the risk represented by processing operations.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_36"></a>Article 36</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Prior consultation</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The controller shall consult the supervisory authority prior to processing where a data protection impact assessment under Article 35 indicates that the processing would result in a high risk in the absence of measures taken by the controller to mitigate the risk.</p>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where the supervisory authority is of the opinion that the intended processing referred to in paragraph&nbsp;1 would infringe this Regulation, in particular where the controller has insufficiently identified or mitigated the risk, the supervisory authority shall, within period of up to eight weeks of receipt of the request for consultation, provide written advice to the controller and, where applicable to the processor, and may use any of its powers referred to in Article&nbsp;58. That period may be extended by six weeks, taking into account the complexity of the intended processing. The supervisory authority shall inform the controller and, where applicable, the processor, of any such extension within one month of receipt of the request for consultation together with the reasons for the delay. Those periods may be suspended until the supervisory authority has obtained information it has requested for the purposes of the consultation.</p>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;When consulting the supervisory authority pursuant to paragraph&nbsp;1, the controller shall provide the supervisory authority with:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">where applicable, the respective responsibilities of the controller, joint controllers and processors involved in the processing, in particular for processing within a group of undertakings;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the purposes and means of the intended processing;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the measures and safeguards provided to protect the rights and freedoms of data subjects pursuant to this Regulation;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(d)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">where applicable, the contact details of the data protection officer;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(e)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the data protection impact assessment provided for in Article&nbsp;35; and</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(f)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">any other information requested by the supervisory authority.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Member States shall consult the supervisory authority during the preparation of a proposal for a legislative measure to be adopted by a national parliament, or of a regulatory measure based on such a legislative measure, which relates to processing.</p>
<p class="normal">5.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Notwithstanding paragraph&nbsp;1, Member&nbsp;State law may require controllers to consult with, and obtain prior authorisation from, the supervisory authority in relation to processing by a controller for the performance of a task carried out by the controller in the public interest, including processing in relation to social protection and public health.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h3 id="d1e3722-1-1" class="ti-section-1"><span class="expanded">Section 4</span></h3>
<p id="L_2016119EN.01000101-d-013" class="ti-section-2"><strong><span class="bold"><span class="expanded">Data protection officer</span></span></strong></p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_37"></a>Article 37</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Designation of the data protection officer</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The controller and the processor shall designate a data protection officer in any case where:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the processing is carried out by a public authority or body, except for courts acting in their judicial capacity;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the core activities of the controller or the processor consist of processing operations which, by virtue of their nature, their scope and/or their purposes, require regular and systematic monitoring of data subjects on a large scale; or</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the core activities of the controller or the processor consist of processing on a large scale of special categories of data pursuant to Article&nbsp;9 and personal data relating to criminal convictions and offences referred to in Article&nbsp;10.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;A group of undertakings may appoint a single data protection officer provided that a data protection officer is easily accessible from each establishment.</p>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where the controller or the processor is a public authority or body, a single data protection officer may be designated for several such authorities or bodies, taking account of their organisational structure and size.</p>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In cases other than those referred to in paragraph&nbsp;1, the controller or processor or associations and other bodies representing categories of controllers or processors may or, where required by Union or Member State law shall, designate a data protection officer. The data protection officer may act for such associations and other bodies representing controllers or processors.</p>
<p class="normal">5.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The data protection officer shall be designated on the basis of professional qualities and, in particular, expert knowledge of data protection law and practices and the ability to fulfil the tasks referred to in Article&nbsp;39.</p>
<p class="normal">6.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The data protection officer may be a staff member of the controller or processor, or fulfil the tasks on the basis of a service contract.</p>
<p class="normal">7.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The controller or the processor shall publish the contact details of the data protection officer and communicate them to the supervisory authority.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_38"></a>Article 38</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Position of the data protection officer</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The controller and the processor shall ensure that the data protection officer is involved, properly and in a timely manner, in all issues which relate to the protection of personal data.</p>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The controller and processor shall support the data protection officer in performing the tasks referred to in Article&nbsp;39 by providing resources necessary to carry out those tasks and access to personal data and processing operations, and to maintain his or her expert knowledge.</p>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The controller and processor shall ensure that the data protection officer does not receive any instructions regarding the exercise of those tasks. He or she shall not be dismissed or penalised by the controller or the processor for performing his tasks. The data protection officer shall directly report to the highest management level of the controller or the processor.</p>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Data subjects may contact the data protection officer with regard to all issues related to processing of their personal data and to the exercise of their rights under this Regulation.</p>
<p class="normal">5.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The data protection officer shall be bound by secrecy or confidentiality concerning the performance of his or her tasks, in accordance with Union or Member&nbsp;State law.</p>
<p class="normal">6.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The data protection officer may fulfil other tasks and duties. The controller or processor shall ensure that any such tasks and duties do not result in a conflict of interests.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_39"></a>Article 39</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Tasks of the data protection officer</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The data protection officer shall have at least the following tasks:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">to inform and advise the controller or the processor and the employees who carry out processing of their obligations pursuant to this Regulation and to other Union or Member State data protection provisions;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">to monitor compliance with this Regulation, with other Union or Member&nbsp;State data protection provisions and with the policies of the controller or processor in relation to the protection of personal data, including the assignment of responsibilities, awareness-raising and training of staff involved in processing operations, and the related audits;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">to provide advice where requested as regards the data protection impact assessment and monitor its performance pursuant to Article&nbsp;35;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(d)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">to cooperate with the supervisory authority;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(e)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">to act as the contact point for the supervisory authority on issues relating to processing, including the prior consultation referred to in Article&nbsp;36, and to consult, where appropriate, with regard to any other matter.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The data protection officer shall in the performance of his or her tasks have due regard to the risk associated with processing operations, taking into account the nature, scope, context and purposes of processing.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h3 id="d1e3875-1-1" class="ti-section-1"><span class="expanded">Section 5</span></h3>
<p id="L_2016119EN.01000101-d-014" class="ti-section-2"><strong><span class="bold"><span class="expanded">Codes of conduct and certification</span></span></strong></p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_40"></a>Article 40</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Codes of conduct</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Member States, the supervisory authorities, the Board and the Commission shall encourage the drawing up of codes of conduct intended to contribute to the proper application of this Regulation, taking account of the specific features of the various processing sectors and the specific needs of micro, small and medium-sized enterprises.</p>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Associations and other bodies representing categories of controllers or processors may prepare codes of conduct, or amend or extend such codes, for the purpose of specifying the application of this Regulation, such as with regard to:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">fair and transparent processing;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the legitimate interests pursued by controllers in specific contexts;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the collection of personal data;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(d)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the pseudonymisation of personal data;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(e)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the information provided to the public and to data subjects;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(f)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the exercise of the rights of data subjects;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(g)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the information provided to, and the protection of, children, and the manner in which the consent of the holders of parental responsibility over children is to be obtained;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(h)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the measures and procedures referred to in Articles 24 and 25 and the measures to ensure security of processing referred to in Article 32;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(i)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the notification of personal data breaches to supervisory authorities and the communication of such personal data breaches to data subjects;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(j)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the transfer of personal data to third countries or international organisations; or</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(k)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">out-of-court proceedings and other dispute resolution procedures for resolving disputes between controllers and data subjects with regard to processing, without prejudice to the rights of data subjects pursuant to Articles 77 and 79.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In addition to adherence by controllers or processors subject to this Regulation, codes of conduct approved pursuant to paragraph 5 of this Article and having general validity pursuant to paragraph 9 of this Article may also be adhered to by controllers or processors that are not subject to this Regulation pursuant to Article&nbsp;3 in order to provide appropriate safeguards within the framework of personal data transfers to third countries or international organisations under the terms referred to in point (e) of Article&nbsp;46(2). Such controllers or processors shall make binding and enforceable commitments, via contractual or other legally binding instruments, to apply those appropriate safeguards including with regard to the rights of data subjects.</p>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;A code of conduct referred to in paragraph 2 of this Article shall contain mechanisms which enable the body referred to in Article&nbsp;41(1) to carry out the mandatory monitoring of compliance with its provisions by the controllers or processors which undertake to apply it, without prejudice to the tasks and powers of supervisory authorities competent pursuant to Article&nbsp;55 or 56.</p>
<p class="normal">5.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Associations and other bodies referred to in paragraph 2 of this Article which intend to prepare a code of conduct or to amend or extend an existing code shall submit the draft code, amendment or extension to the supervisory authority which is competent pursuant to Article&nbsp;55. The supervisory authority shall provide an opinion on whether the draft code, amendment or extension complies with this Regulation and shall approve that draft code, amendment or extension if it finds that it provides sufficient appropriate safeguards.</p>
<p class="normal">6.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where the draft code, or amendment or extension is approved in accordance with paragraph&nbsp;5, and where the code of conduct concerned does not relate to processing activities in several Member&nbsp;States, the supervisory authority shall register and publish the code.</p>
<p class="normal">7.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where a draft code of conduct relates to processing activities in several Member&nbsp;States, the supervisory authority which is competent pursuant to Article 55 shall, before approving the draft code, amendment or extension, submit it in the procedure referred to in Article&nbsp;63 to the Board which shall provide an opinion on whether the draft code, amendment or extension complies with this Regulation or, in the situation referred to in paragraph&nbsp;3 of this Article, provides appropriate safeguards.</p>
<p class="normal">8.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where the opinion referred to in paragraph 7 confirms that the draft code, amendment or extension complies with this Regulation, or, in the situation referred to in paragraph&nbsp;3, provides appropriate safeguards, the Board shall submit its opinion to the Commission.</p>
<p class="normal">9.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Commission may, by way of implementing acts, decide that the approved code of conduct, amendment or extension submitted to it pursuant to paragraph&nbsp;8 of this Article have general validity within the Union. Those implementing acts shall be adopted in accordance with the examination procedure set out in Article&nbsp;93(2).</p>
<p class="normal">10.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Commission shall ensure appropriate publicity for the approved codes which have been decided as having general validity in accordance with paragraph 9.</p>
<p class="normal">11.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Board shall collate all approved codes of conduct, amendments and extensions in a register and shall make them publicly available by way of appropriate means.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_41"></a>Article 41</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Monitoring of approved codes of conduct</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Without prejudice to the tasks and powers of the competent supervisory authority under Articles&nbsp;57 and 58, the monitoring of compliance with a code of conduct pursuant to Article&nbsp;40 may be carried out by a body which has an appropriate level of expertise in relation to the subject-matter of the code and is accredited for that purpose by the competent supervisory authority.</p>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;A body as referred to in paragraph&nbsp;1 may be accredited to monitor compliance with a code of conduct where that body has:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">demonstrated its independence and expertise in relation to the subject-matter of the code to the satisfaction of the competent supervisory authority;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">established procedures which allow it to assess the eligibility of controllers and processors concerned to apply the code, to monitor their compliance with its provisions and to periodically review its operation;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">established procedures and structures to handle complaints about infringements of the code or the manner in which the code has been, or is being, implemented by a controller or processor, and to make those procedures and structures transparent to data subjects and the public; and</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(d)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">demonstrated to the satisfaction of the competent supervisory authority that its tasks and duties do not result in a conflict of interests.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The competent supervisory authority shall submit the draft criteria for accreditation of a body as referred to in paragraph 1 of this Article to the Board pursuant to the consistency mechanism referred to in Article&nbsp;63.</p>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Without prejudice to the tasks and powers of the competent supervisory authority and the provisions of Chapter&nbsp;VIII, a body as referred to in paragraph 1 of this Article shall, subject to appropriate safeguards, take appropriate action in cases of infringement of the code by a controller or processor, including suspension or exclusion of the controller or processor concerned from the code. It shall inform the competent supervisory authority of such actions and the reasons for taking them.</p>
<p class="normal">5.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The competent supervisory authority shall revoke the accreditation of a body as referred to in paragraph&nbsp;1 if the conditions for accreditation are not, or are no longer, met or where actions taken by the body infringe this Regulation.</p>
<p class="normal">6.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;This Article shall not apply to processing carried out by public authorities and bodies.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_42"></a>Article 42</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Certification</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Member States, the supervisory authorities, the Board and the Commission shall encourage, in particular at Union level, the establishment of data protection certification mechanisms and of data protection seals and marks, for the purpose of demonstrating compliance with this Regulation of processing operations by controllers and processors. The specific needs of micro, small and medium-sized enterprises shall be taken into account.</p>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In addition to adherence by controllers or processors subject to this Regulation, data protection certification mechanisms, seals or marks approved pursuant to paragraph&nbsp;5 of this Article may be established for the purpose of demonstrating the existence of appropriate safeguards provided by controllers or processors that are not subject to this Regulation pursuant to Article&nbsp;3 within the framework of personal data transfers to third countries or international organisations under the terms referred to in point&nbsp;(f) of Article&nbsp;46(2). Such controllers or processors shall make binding and enforceable commitments, via contractual or other legally binding instruments, to apply those appropriate safeguards, including with regard to the rights of data subjects.</p>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The certification shall be voluntary and available via a process that is transparent.</p>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;A certification pursuant to this Article does not reduce the responsibility of the controller or the processor for compliance with this Regulation and is without prejudice to the tasks and powers of the supervisory authorities which are competent pursuant to Article&nbsp;55 or&nbsp;56.</p>
<p class="normal">5.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;A certification pursuant to this Article shall be issued by the certification bodies referred to in Article&nbsp;43 or by the competent supervisory authority, on the basis of criteria approved by that competent supervisory authority pursuant to Article&nbsp;58(3) or by the Board pursuant to Article&nbsp;63. Where the criteria are approved by the Board, this may result in a common certification, the European Data Protection Seal.</p>
<p class="normal">6.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The controller or processor which submits its processing to the certification mechanism shall provide the certification body referred to in Article&nbsp;43, or where applicable, the competent supervisory authority, with all information and access to its processing activities which are necessary to conduct the certification procedure.</p>
<p class="normal">7.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Certification shall be issued to a controller or processor for a maximum period of three years and may be renewed, under the same conditions, provided that the relevant requirements continue to be met. Certification shall be withdrawn, as applicable, by the certification bodies referred to in Article&nbsp;43 or by the competent supervisory authority where the requirements for the certification are not or are no longer met.</p>
<p class="normal">8.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Board shall collate all certification mechanisms and data protection seals and marks in a register and shall make them publicly available by any appropriate means.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_43"></a>Article 43</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Certification bodies</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Without prejudice to the tasks and powers of the competent supervisory authority under Articles&nbsp;57 and 58, certification bodies which have an appropriate level of expertise in relation to data protection shall, after informing the supervisory authority in order to allow it to exercise its powers pursuant to point (h) of Article&nbsp;58(2) where necessary, issue and renew certification. Member States shall ensure that those certification bodies are accredited by one or both of the following:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the supervisory authority which is competent pursuant to Article&nbsp;55 or 56;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the national accreditation body named in accordance with Regulation (EC) No&nbsp;765/2008 of the European Parliament and of the Council<a id="ntc20-L_2016119EN.01000101-E0020" href="https://ogdpr.eu/en/gdpr-2016-679#regula_sources">&nbsp;(<span class="super">20</span>)</a>&nbsp;in accordance with EN-ISO/IEC 17065/2012 and with the additional requirements established by the supervisory authority which is competent pursuant to Article&nbsp;55 or&nbsp;56.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Certification bodies referred to in paragraph&nbsp;1 shall be accredited in accordance with that paragraph only where they have:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">demonstrated their independence and expertise in relation to the subject-matter of the certification to the satisfaction of the competent supervisory authority;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">undertaken to respect the criteria referred to in Article&nbsp;42(5) and approved by the supervisory authority which is competent pursuant to Article&nbsp;55 or&nbsp;56 or by the Board pursuant to Article&nbsp;63;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">established procedures for the issuing, periodic review and withdrawal of data protection certification, seals and marks;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(d)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">established procedures and structures to handle complaints about infringements of the certification or the manner in which the certification has been, or is being, implemented by the controller or processor, and to make those procedures and structures transparent to data subjects and the public; and</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(e)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">demonstrated, to the satisfaction of the competent supervisory authority, that their tasks and duties do not result in a conflict of interests.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The accreditation of certification bodies as referred to in paragraphs&nbsp;1 and 2 of this Article shall take place on the basis of criteria approved by the supervisory authority which is competent pursuant to Article&nbsp;55 or 56 or by the Board pursuant to Article&nbsp;63. In the case of accreditation pursuant to point&nbsp;(b) of paragraph&nbsp;1 of this Article, those requirements shall complement those envisaged in Regulation (EC) No&nbsp;765/2008 and the technical rules that describe the methods and procedures of the certification bodies.</p>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The certification bodies referred to in paragraph&nbsp;1 shall be responsible for the proper assessment leading to the certification or the withdrawal of such certification without prejudice to the responsibility of the controller or processor for compliance with this Regulation. The accreditation shall be issued for a maximum period of five years and may be renewed on the same conditions provided that the certification body meets the requirements set out in this Article.</p>
<p class="normal">5.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The certification bodies referred to in paragraph&nbsp;1 shall provide the competent supervisory authorities with the reasons for granting or withdrawing the requested certification.</p>
<p class="normal">6.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The requirements referred to in paragraph&nbsp;3 of this Article and the criteria referred to in Article&nbsp;42(5) shall be made public by the supervisory authority in an easily accessible form. The supervisory authorities shall also transmit those requirements and criteria to the Board. The Board shall collate all certification mechanisms and data protection seals in a register and shall make them publicly available by any appropriate means.</p>
<p class="normal">7.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Without prejudice to Chapter VIII, the competent supervisory authority or the national accreditation body shall revoke an accreditation of a certification body pursuant to paragraph&nbsp;1 of this Article where the conditions for the accreditation are not, or are no longer, met or where actions taken by a certification body infringe this Regulation.</p>
<p class="normal">8.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Commission shall be empowered to adopt delegated acts in accordance with Article&nbsp;92 for the purpose of specifying the requirements to be taken into account for the data protection certification mechanisms referred to in Article&nbsp;42(1).</p>
<p class="normal">9.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Commission may adopt implementing acts laying down technical standards for certification mechanisms and data protection seals and marks, and mechanisms to promote and recognise those certification mechanisms, seals and marks. Those implementing acts shall be adopted in accordance with the examination procedure referred to in Article&nbsp;93(2).</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h2 id="d1e4227-1-1" class="ti-section-1"><span class="italic">CHAPTER V</span></h2>
<p id="L_2016119EN.01000101-d-015" class="ti-section-2"><strong><span class="bold"><span class="italic">Transfers of personal data to third countries or international organisations</span></span></strong></p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_44"></a>Article 44</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>General principle for transfers</strong></p>
<p class="normal">Any transfer of personal data which are undergoing processing or are intended for processing after transfer to a third country or to an international organisation shall take place only if, subject to the other provisions of this Regulation, the conditions laid down in this Chapter are complied with by the controller and processor, including for onward transfers of personal data from the third country or an international organisation to another third country or to another international organisation. All provisions in this Chapter shall be applied in order to ensure that the level of protection of natural persons guaranteed by this Regulation is not undermined.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_45"></a>Article 45</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Transfers on the basis of an adequacy decision</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;A transfer of personal data to a third country or an international organisation may take place where the Commission has decided that the third country, a territory or one or more specified sectors within that third country, or the international organisation in question ensures an adequate level of protection. Such a transfer shall not require any specific authorisation.</p>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;When assessing the adequacy of the level of protection, the Commission shall, in particular, take account of the following elements:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the rule of law, respect for human rights and fundamental freedoms, relevant legislation, both general and sectoral, including concerning public security, defence, national security and criminal law and the access of public authorities to personal data, as well as the implementation of such legislation, data protection rules, professional rules and security measures, including rules for the onward transfer of personal data to another third country or international organisation which are complied with in that country or international organisation, case-law, as well as effective and enforceable data subject rights and effective administrative and judicial redress for the data subjects whose personal data are being transferred;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the existence and effective functioning of one or more independent supervisory authorities in the third country or to which an international organisation is subject, with responsibility for ensuring and enforcing compliance with the data protection rules, including adequate enforcement powers, for assisting and advising the data subjects in exercising their rights and for cooperation with the supervisory authorities of the Member&nbsp;States; and</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the international commitments the third country or international organisation concerned has entered into, or other obligations arising from legally binding conventions or instruments as well as from its participation in multilateral or regional systems, in particular in relation to the protection of personal data.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Commission, after assessing the adequacy of the level of protection, may decide, by means of implementing act, that a third country, a territory or one or more specified sectors within a third country, or an international organisation ensures an adequate level of protection within the meaning of paragraph&nbsp;2 of this Article. The implementing act shall provide for a mechanism for a periodic review, at least every four years, which shall take into account all relevant developments in the third country or international organisation. The implementing act shall specify its territorial and sectoral application and, where applicable, identify the supervisory authority or authorities referred to in point (b) of paragraph 2 of this Article. The implementing act shall be adopted in accordance with the examination procedure referred to in Article 93(2).</p>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Commission shall, on an ongoing basis, monitor developments in third countries and international organisations that could affect the functioning of decisions adopted pursuant to paragraph&nbsp;3 of this Article and decisions adopted on the basis of Article&nbsp;25(6) of Directive 95/46/EC.</p>
<p class="normal">5.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Commission shall, where available information reveals, in particular following the review referred to in paragraph 3 of this Article, that a third country, a territory or one or more specified sectors within a third country, or an international organisation no longer ensures an adequate level of protection within the meaning of paragraph&nbsp;2 of this Article, to the extent necessary, repeal, amend or suspend the decision referred to in paragraph&nbsp;3 of this Article by means of implementing acts without retro-active effect. Those implementing acts shall be adopted in accordance with the examination procedure referred to in Article&nbsp;93(2).</p>
<p class="normal">On duly justified imperative grounds of urgency, the Commission shall adopt immediately applicable implementing acts in accordance with the procedure referred to in Article&nbsp;93(3).</p>
<p class="normal">6.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Commission shall enter into consultations with the third country or international organisation with a view to remedying the situation giving rise to the decision made pursuant to paragraph&nbsp;5.</p>
<p class="normal">7.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;A decision pursuant to paragraph&nbsp;5 of this Article is without prejudice to transfers of personal data to the third country, a territory or one or more specified sectors within that third country, or the international organisation in question pursuant to Articles&nbsp;46 to 49.</p>
<p class="normal">8.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Commission shall publish in the&nbsp;<span class="italic">Official Journal of the European Union</span>&nbsp;and on its website a list of the third countries, territories and specified sectors within a third country and international organisations for which it has decided that an adequate level of protection is or is no longer ensured.</p>
<p class="normal">9.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Decisions adopted by the Commission on the basis of Article&nbsp;25(6) of Directive&nbsp;95/46/EC shall remain in force until amended, replaced or repealed by a Commission Decision adopted in accordance with paragraph&nbsp;3 or 5 of this Article.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_46"></a>Article 46</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Transfers subject to appropriate safeguards</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In the absence of a decision pursuant to Article 45(3), a controller or processor may transfer personal data to a third country or an international organisation only if the controller or processor has provided appropriate safeguards, and on condition that enforceable data subject rights and effective legal remedies for data subjects are available.</p>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The appropriate safeguards referred to in paragraph 1 may be provided for, without requiring any specific authorisation from a supervisory authority, by:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">a legally binding and enforceable instrument between public authorities or bodies;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">binding corporate rules in accordance with Article 47;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">standard data protection clauses adopted by the Commission in accordance with the examination procedure referred to in Article 93(2);</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(d)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">standard data protection clauses adopted by a supervisory authority and approved by the Commission pursuant to the examination procedure referred to in Article&nbsp;93(2);</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(e)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">an approved code of conduct pursuant to Article 40 together with binding and enforceable commitments of the controller or processor in the third country to apply the appropriate safeguards, including as regards data subjects’ rights; or</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(f)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">an approved certification mechanism pursuant to Article&nbsp;42 together with binding and enforceable commitments of the controller or processor in the third country to apply the appropriate safeguards, including as regards data subjects’ rights.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Subject to the authorisation from the competent supervisory authority, the appropriate safeguards referred to in paragraph&nbsp;1 may also be provided for, in particular, by:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">contractual clauses between the controller or processor and the controller, processor or the recipient of the personal data in the third country or international organisation; or</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">provisions to be inserted into administrative arrangements between public authorities or bodies which include enforceable and effective data subject rights.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The supervisory authority shall apply the consistency mechanism referred to in Article&nbsp;63 in the cases referred to in paragraph&nbsp;3 of this Article.</p>
<p class="normal">5.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Authorisations by a Member State or supervisory authority on the basis of Article&nbsp;26(2) of Directive 95/46/EC shall remain valid until amended, replaced or repealed, if necessary, by that supervisory authority. Decisions adopted by the Commission on the basis of Article&nbsp;26(4) of Directive&nbsp;95/46/EC shall remain in force until amended, replaced or repealed, if necessary, by a Commission Decision adopted in accordance with paragraph&nbsp;2 of this Article.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_47"></a>Article 47</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Binding corporate rules</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The competent supervisory authority shall approve binding corporate rules in accordance with the consistency mechanism set out in Article 63, provided that they:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">are legally binding and apply to and are enforced by every member concerned of the group of undertakings, or group of enterprises engaged in a joint economic activity, including their employees;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">expressly confer enforceable rights on data subjects with regard to the processing of their personal data; and</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">fulfil the requirements laid down in paragraph&nbsp;2.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The binding corporate rules referred to in paragraph&nbsp;1 shall specify at least:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the structure and contact details of the group of undertakings, or group of enterprises engaged in a joint economic activity and of each of its members;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the data transfers or set of transfers, including the categories of personal data, the type of processing and its purposes, the type of data subjects affected and the identification of the third country or countries in question;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">their legally binding nature, both internally and externally;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(d)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the application of the general data protection principles, in particular purpose limitation, data minimisation, limited storage periods, data quality, data protection by design and by default, legal basis for processing, processing of special categories of personal data, measures to ensure data security, and the requirements in respect of onward transfers to bodies not bound by the binding corporate rules;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(e)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the rights of data subjects in regard to processing and the means to exercise those rights, including the right not to be subject to decisions based solely on automated processing, including profiling in accordance with Article&nbsp;22, the right to lodge a complaint with the competent supervisory authority and before the competent courts of the Member States in accordance with Article&nbsp;79, and to obtain redress and, where appropriate, compensation for a breach of the binding corporate rules;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(f)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the acceptance by the controller or processor established on the territory of a Member&nbsp;State of liability for any breaches of the binding corporate rules by any member concerned not established in the Union; the controller or the processor shall be exempt from that liability, in whole or in part, only if it proves that that member is not responsible for the event giving rise to the damage;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(g)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">how the information on the binding corporate rules, in particular on the provisions referred to in points (d), (e) and&nbsp;(f) of this paragraph is provided to the data subjects in addition to Articles&nbsp;13 and 14;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(h)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the tasks of any data protection officer designated in accordance with Article&nbsp;37 or any other person or entity in charge of the monitoring compliance with the binding corporate rules within the group of undertakings, or group of enterprises engaged in a joint economic activity, as well as monitoring training and complaint-handling;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(i)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the complaint procedures;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(j)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the mechanisms within the group of undertakings, or group of enterprises engaged in a joint economic activity for ensuring the verification of compliance with the binding corporate rules. Such mechanisms shall include data protection audits and methods for ensuring corrective actions to protect the rights of the data subject. Results of such verification should be communicated to the person or entity referred to in point&nbsp;(h) and to the board of the controlling undertaking of a group of undertakings, or of the group of enterprises engaged in a joint economic activity, and should be available upon request to the competent supervisory authority;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(k)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the mechanisms for reporting and recording changes to the rules and reporting those changes to the supervisory authority;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(l)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the cooperation mechanism with the supervisory authority to ensure compliance by any member of the group of undertakings, or group of enterprises engaged in a joint economic activity, in particular by making available to the supervisory authority the results of verifications of the measures referred to in point (j);</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(m)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the mechanisms for reporting to the competent supervisory authority any legal requirements to which a member of the group of undertakings, or group of enterprises engaged in a joint economic activity is subject in a third country which are likely to have a substantial adverse effect on the guarantees provided by the binding corporate rules; and</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(n)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the appropriate data protection training to personnel having permanent or regular access to personal data.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Commission may specify the format and procedures for the exchange of information between controllers, processors and supervisory authorities for binding corporate rules within the meaning of this Article. Those implementing acts shall be adopted in accordance with the examination procedure set out in Article&nbsp;93(2).</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_48"></a>Article 48</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Transfers or disclosures not authorised by Union law</strong></p>
<p class="normal">Any judgment of a court or tribunal and any decision of an administrative authority of a third country requiring a controller or processor to transfer or disclose personal data may only be recognised or enforceable in any manner if based on an international agreement, such as a mutual legal assistance treaty, in force between the requesting third country and the Union or a Member&nbsp;State, without prejudice to other grounds for transfer pursuant to this Chapter.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_49"></a>Article 49</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Derogations for specific situations</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In the absence of an adequacy decision pursuant to Article&nbsp;45(3), or of appropriate safeguards pursuant to Article&nbsp;46, including binding corporate rules, a transfer or a set of transfers of personal data to a third country or an international organisation shall take place only on one of the following conditions:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
