<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the data subject has explicitly consented to the proposed transfer, after having been informed of the possible risks of such transfers for the data subject due to the absence of an adequacy decision and appropriate safeguards;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the transfer is necessary for the performance of a contract between the data subject and the controller or the implementation of pre-contractual measures taken at the data subject’s request;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the transfer is necessary for the conclusion or performance of a contract concluded in the interest of the data subject between the controller and another natural or legal person;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(d)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the transfer is necessary for important reasons of public interest;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(e)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the transfer is necessary for the establishment, exercise or defence of legal claims;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(f)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the transfer is necessary in order to protect the vital interests of the data subject or of other persons, where the data subject is physically or legally incapable of giving consent;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(g)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the transfer is made from a register which according to Union or Member State law is intended to provide information to the public and which is open to consultation either by the public in general or by any person who can demonstrate a legitimate interest, but only to the extent that the conditions laid down by Union or Member&nbsp;State law for consultation are fulfilled in the particular case.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">Where a transfer could not be based on a provision in Article 45 or 46, including the provisions on binding corporate rules, and none of the derogations for a specific situation referred to in the first subparagraph of this paragraph is applicable, a transfer to a third country or an international organisation may take place only if the transfer is not repetitive, concerns only a limited number of data subjects, is necessary for the purposes of compelling legitimate interests pursued by the controller which are not overridden by the interests or rights and freedoms of the data subject, and the controller has assessed all the circumstances surrounding the data transfer and has on the basis of that assessment provided suitable safeguards with regard to the protection of personal data. The controller shall inform the supervisory authority of the transfer. The controller shall, in addition to providing the information referred to in Articles&nbsp;13 and 14, inform the data subject of the transfer and on the compelling legitimate interests pursued.</p>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;A transfer pursuant to point (g) of the first subparagraph of paragraph 1 shall not involve the entirety of the personal data or entire categories of the personal data contained in the register. Where the register is intended for consultation by persons having a legitimate interest, the transfer shall be made only at the request of those persons or if they are to be the recipients.</p>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Points (a), (b) and (c) of the first subparagraph of paragraph 1 and the second subparagraph thereof shall not apply to activities carried out by public authorities in the exercise of their public powers.</p>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The public interest referred to in point (d) of the first subparagraph of paragraph 1 shall be recognised in Union law or in the law of the Member State to which the controller is subject.</p>
<p class="normal">5.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In the absence of an adequacy decision, Union or Member State law may, for important reasons of public interest, expressly set limits to the transfer of specific categories of personal data to a third country or an international organisation. Member States shall notify such provisions to the Commission.</p>
<p class="normal">6.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The controller or processor shall document the assessment as well as the suitable safeguards referred to in the second subparagraph of paragraph&nbsp;1 of this Article in the records referred to in Article 30.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_50"></a>Article 50</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>International cooperation for the protection of personal data</strong></p>
<p class="normal">In relation to third countries and international organisations, the Commission and supervisory authorities shall take appropriate steps to:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">develop international cooperation mechanisms to facilitate the effective enforcement of legislation for the protection of personal data;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">provide international mutual assistance in the enforcement of legislation for the protection of personal data, including through notification, complaint referral, investigative assistance and information exchange, subject to appropriate safeguards for the protection of personal data and other fundamental rights and freedoms;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">engage relevant stakeholders in discussion and activities aimed at furthering international cooperation in the enforcement of legislation for the protection of personal data;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(d)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">promote the exchange and documentation of personal data protection legislation and practice, including on jurisdictional conflicts with third countries.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h2 id="d1e4650-1-1" class="ti-section-1"><span class="italic">CHAPTER VI</span></h2>
<p id="L_2016119EN.01000101-d-016" class="ti-section-2"><strong><span class="bold"><span class="italic">Independent supervisory authorities</span></span></strong></p>
<h3 id="d1e4661-1-1" class="ti-section-1"><span class="expanded">Section 1</span></h3>
<p id="L_2016119EN.01000101-d-017" class="ti-section-2"><strong><span class="bold"><span class="expanded">Independent status</span></span></strong></p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_51"></a>Article 51</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Supervisory authority</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Each Member State shall provide for one or more independent public authorities to be responsible for monitoring the application of this Regulation, in order to protect the fundamental rights and freedoms of natural persons in relation to processing and to facilitate the free flow of personal data within the Union (‘supervisory authority’).</p>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Each supervisory authority shall contribute to the consistent application of this Regulation throughout the Union. For that purpose, the supervisory authorities shall cooperate with each other and the Commission in accordance with Chapter VII.</p>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where more than one supervisory authority is established in a Member State, that Member&nbsp;State shall designate the supervisory authority which is to represent those authorities in the Board and shall set out the mechanism to ensure compliance by the other authorities with the rules relating to the consistency mechanism referred to in Article&nbsp;63.</p>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Each Member State shall notify to the Commission the provisions of its law which it adopts pursuant to this Chapter, by 25 May 2018 and, without delay, any subsequent amendment affecting them.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_52"></a>Article 52</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Independence</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Each supervisory authority shall act with complete independence in performing its tasks and exercising its powers in accordance with this Regulation.</p>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The member or members of each supervisory authority shall, in the performance of their tasks and exercise of their powers in accordance with this Regulation, remain free from external influence, whether direct or indirect, and shall neither seek nor take instructions from anybody.</p>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Member or members of each supervisory authority shall refrain from any action incompatible with their duties and shall not, during their term of office, engage in any incompatible occupation, whether gainful or not.</p>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Each Member State shall ensure that each supervisory authority is provided with the human, technical and financial resources, premises and infrastructure necessary for the effective performance of its tasks and exercise of its powers, including those to be carried out in the context of mutual assistance, cooperation and participation in the Board.</p>
<p class="normal">5.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Each Member State shall ensure that each supervisory authority chooses and has its own staff which shall be subject to the exclusive direction of the member or members of the supervisory authority concerned.</p>
<p class="normal">6.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Each Member State shall ensure that each supervisory authority is subject to financial control which does not affect its independence and that it has separate, public annual budgets, which may be part of the overall state or national budget.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_53"></a>Article 53</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>General conditions for the members of the supervisory authority</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Member States shall provide for each member of their supervisory authorities to be appointed by means of a transparent procedure by:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">—</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">their parliament;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">—</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">their government;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">—</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">their head of State; or</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">—</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">an independent body entrusted with the appointment under Member State law.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Each member shall have the qualifications, experience and skills, in particular in the area of the protection of personal data, required to perform its duties and exercise its powers.</p>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The duties of a member shall end in the event of the expiry of the term of office, resignation or compulsory retirement, in accordance with the law of the Member&nbsp;State concerned.</p>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;A member shall be dismissed only in cases of serious misconduct or if the member no longer fulfils the conditions required for the performance of the duties.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_54"></a>Article 54</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Rules on the establishment of the supervisory authority</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Each Member State shall provide by law for all of the following:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the establishment of each supervisory authority;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the qualifications and eligibility conditions required to be appointed as member of each supervisory authority;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the rules and procedures for the appointment of the member or members of each supervisory authority;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(d)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the duration of the term of the member or members of each supervisory authority of no less than four years, except for the first appointment after 24 May 2016, part of which may take place for a shorter period where that is necessary to protect the independence of the supervisory authority by means of a staggered appointment procedure;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(e)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">whether and, if so, for how many terms the member or members of each supervisory authority is eligible for reappointment;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(f)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the conditions governing the obligations of the member or members and staff of each supervisory authority, prohibitions on actions, occupations and benefits incompatible therewith during and after the term of office and rules governing the cessation of employment.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The member or members and the staff of each supervisory authority shall, in accordance with Union or Member State law, be subject to a duty of professional secrecy both during and after their term of office, with regard to any confidential information which has come to their knowledge in the course of the performance of their tasks or exercise of their powers. During their term of office, that duty of professional secrecy shall in particular apply to reporting by natural persons of infringements of this Regulation.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h3 id="d1e4834-1-1" class="ti-section-1"><span class="expanded">Section 2</span></h3>
<p id="L_2016119EN.01000101-d-018" class="ti-section-2"><strong><span class="bold"><span class="expanded">Competence, tasks and powers</span></span></strong></p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_55"></a>Article 55</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Competence</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Each supervisory authority shall be competent for the performance of the tasks assigned to and the exercise of the powers conferred on it in accordance with this Regulation on the territory of its own Member State.</p>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where processing is carried out by public authorities or private bodies acting on the basis of point&nbsp;(c) or (e) of Article 6(1), the supervisory authority of the Member&nbsp;State concerned shall be competent. In such cases Article 56 does not apply.</p>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Supervisory authorities shall not be competent to supervise processing operations of courts acting in their judicial capacity.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_56"></a>Article 56</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Competence of the lead supervisory authority</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Without prejudice to Article 55, the supervisory authority of the main establishment or of the single establishment of the controller or processor shall be competent to act as lead supervisory authority for the cross-border processing carried out by that controller or processor in accordance with the procedure provided in Article 60.</p>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;By derogation from paragraph 1, each supervisory authority shall be competent to handle a complaint lodged with it or a possible infringement of this Regulation, if the subject matter relates only to an establishment in its Member State or substantially affects data subjects only in its Member State.</p>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In the cases referred to in paragraph 2 of this Article, the supervisory authority shall inform the lead supervisory authority without delay on that matter. Within a period of three weeks after being informed the lead supervisory authority shall decide whether or not it will handle the case in accordance with the procedure provided in Article 60, taking into account whether or not there is an establishment of the controller or processor in the Member State of which the supervisory authority informed it.</p>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where the lead supervisory authority decides to handle the case, the procedure provided in Article 60 shall apply. The supervisory authority which informed the lead supervisory authority may submit to the lead supervisory authority a draft for a decision. The lead supervisory authority shall take utmost account of that draft when preparing the draft decision referred to in Article 60(3).</p>
<p class="normal">5.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where the lead supervisory authority decides not to handle the case, the supervisory authority which informed the lead supervisory authority shall handle it according to Articles&nbsp;61 and 62.</p>
<p class="normal">6.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The lead supervisory authority shall be the sole interlocutor of the controller or processor for the cross-border processing carried out by that controller or processor.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_57"></a>Article 57</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Tasks</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Without prejudice to other tasks set out under this Regulation, each supervisory authority shall on its territory:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">monitor and enforce the application of this Regulation;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">promote public awareness and understanding of the risks, rules, safeguards and rights in relation to processing. Activities addressed specifically to children shall receive specific attention;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">advise, in accordance with Member State law, the national parliament, the government, and other institutions and bodies on legislative and administrative measures relating to the protection of natural persons’ rights and freedoms with regard to processing;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(d)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">promote the awareness of controllers and processors of their obligations under this Regulation;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(e)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">upon request, provide information to any data subject concerning the exercise of their rights under this Regulation and, if appropriate, cooperate with the supervisory authorities in other Member States to that end;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(f)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">handle complaints lodged by a data subject, or by a body, organisation or association in accordance with Article&nbsp;80, and investigate, to the extent appropriate, the subject matter of the complaint and inform the complainant of the progress and the outcome of the investigation within a reasonable period, in particular if further investigation or coordination with another supervisory authority is necessary;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(g)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">cooperate with, including sharing information and provide mutual assistance to, other supervisory authorities with a view to ensuring the consistency of application and enforcement of this Regulation;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(h)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">conduct investigations on the application of this Regulation, including on the basis of information received from another supervisory authority or other public authority;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(i)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">monitor relevant developments, insofar as they have an impact on the protection of personal data, in particular the development of information and communication technologies and commercial practices;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(j)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">adopt standard contractual clauses referred to in Article&nbsp;28(8) and in point&nbsp;(d) of Article&nbsp;46(2);</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(k)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">establish and maintain a list in relation to the requirement for data protection impact assessment pursuant to Article&nbsp;35(4);</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(l)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">give advice on the processing operations referred to in Article 36(2);</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(m)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">encourage the drawing up of codes of conduct pursuant to Article&nbsp;40(1) and provide an opinion and approve such codes of conduct which provide sufficient safeguards, pursuant to Article&nbsp;40(5);</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(n)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">encourage the establishment of data protection certification mechanisms and of data protection seals and marks pursuant to Article&nbsp;42(1), and approve the criteria of certification pursuant to Article&nbsp;42(5);</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(o)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">where applicable, carry out a periodic review of certifications issued in accordance with Article&nbsp;42(7);</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(p)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">draft and publish the criteria for accreditation of a body for monitoring codes of conduct pursuant to Article&nbsp;41 and of a certification body pursuant to Article&nbsp;43;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(q)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">conduct the accreditation of a body for monitoring codes of conduct pursuant to Article&nbsp;41 and of a certification body pursuant to Article&nbsp;43;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(r)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">authorise contractual clauses and provisions referred to in Article&nbsp;46(3);</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(s)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">approve binding corporate rules pursuant to Article&nbsp;47;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(t)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">contribute to the activities of the Board;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(u)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">keep internal records of infringements of this Regulation and of measures taken in accordance with Article&nbsp;58(2); and</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(v)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">fulfil any other tasks related to the protection of personal data.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Each supervisory authority shall facilitate the submission of complaints referred to in point&nbsp;(f) of paragraph 1 by measures such as a complaint submission form which can also be completed electronically, without excluding other means of communication.</p>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The performance of the tasks of each supervisory authority shall be free of charge for the data subject and, where applicable, for the data protection officer.</p>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where requests are manifestly unfounded or excessive, in particular because of their repetitive character, the supervisory authority may charge a reasonable fee based on administrative costs, or refuse to act on the request. The supervisory authority shall bear the burden of demonstrating the manifestly unfounded or excessive character of the request.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_58"></a>Article 58</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Powers</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Each supervisory authority shall have all of the following investigative powers:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">to order the controller and the processor, and, where applicable, the controller’s or the processor’s representative to provide any information it requires for the performance of its tasks;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">to carry out investigations in the form of data protection audits;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">to carry out a review on certifications issued pursuant to Article&nbsp;42(7);</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(d)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">to notify the controller or the processor of an alleged infringement of this Regulation;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(e)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">to obtain, from the controller and the processor, access to all personal data and to all information necessary for the performance of its tasks;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(f)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">to obtain access to any premises of the controller and the processor, including to any data processing equipment and means, in accordance with Union or Member&nbsp;State procedural law.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Each supervisory authority shall have all of the following corrective powers:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">to issue warnings to a controller or processor that intended processing operations are likely to infringe provisions of this Regulation;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">to issue reprimands to a controller or a processor where processing operations have infringed provisions of this Regulation;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">to order the controller or the processor to comply with the data subject’s requests to exercise his or her rights pursuant to this Regulation;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(d)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">to order the controller or processor to bring processing operations into compliance with the provisions of this Regulation, where appropriate, in a specified manner and within a specified period;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(e)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">to order the controller to communicate a personal data breach to the data subject;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(f)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">to impose a temporary or definitive limitation including a ban on processing;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(g)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">to order the rectification or erasure of personal data or restriction of processing pursuant to Articles&nbsp;16, 17 and 18 and the notification of such actions to recipients to whom the personal data have been disclosed pursuant to Article&nbsp;17(2) and Article 19;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(h)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">to withdraw a certification or to order the certification body to withdraw a certification issued pursuant to Articles&nbsp;42 and 43, or to order the certification body not to issue certification if the requirements for the certification are not or are no longer met;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(i)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">to impose an administrative fine pursuant to Article 83, in addition to, or instead of measures referred to in this paragraph, depending on the circumstances of each individual case;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(j)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">to order the suspension of data flows to a recipient in a third country or to an international organisation.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Each supervisory authority shall have all of the following authorisation and advisory powers:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">to advise the controller in accordance with the prior consultation procedure referred to in Article 36;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">to issue, on its own initiative or on request, opinions to the national parliament, the Member State government or, in accordance with Member State law, to other institutions and bodies as well as to the public on any issue related to the protection of personal data;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">to authorise processing referred to in Article 36(5), if the law of the Member State requires such prior authorisation;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(d)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">to issue an opinion and approve draft codes of conduct pursuant to Article 40(5);</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(e)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">to accredit certification bodies pursuant to Article 43;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(f)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">to issue certifications and approve criteria of certification in accordance with Article&nbsp;42(5);</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(g)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">to adopt standard data protection clauses referred to in Article 28(8) and in point&nbsp;(d) of Article 46(2);</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(h)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">to authorise contractual clauses referred to in point (a) of Article 46(3);</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(i)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">to authorise administrative arrangements referred to in point (b) of Article 46(3);</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(j)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">to approve binding corporate rules pursuant to Article 47.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The exercise of the powers conferred on the supervisory authority pursuant to this Article shall be subject to appropriate safeguards, including effective judicial remedy and due process, set out in Union and Member&nbsp;State law in accordance with the Charter.</p>
<p class="normal">5.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Each Member&nbsp;State shall provide by law that its supervisory authority shall have the power to bring infringements of this Regulation to the attention of the judicial authorities and where appropriate, to commence or engage otherwise in legal proceedings, in order to enforce the provisions of this Regulation.</p>
<p class="normal">6.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Each Member State may provide by law that its supervisory authority shall have additional powers to those referred to in paragraphs&nbsp;1, 2 and 3. The exercise of those powers shall not impair the effective operation of Chapter&nbsp;VII.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_59"></a>Article 59</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Activity reports</strong></p>
<p class="normal">Each supervisory authority shall draw up an annual report on its activities, which may include a list of types of infringement notified and types of measures taken in accordance with Article&nbsp;58(2). Those reports shall be transmitted to the national parliament, the government and other authorities as designated by Member&nbsp;State law. They shall be made available to the public, to the Commission and to the Board.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h2 id="d1e5264-1-1" class="ti-section-1"><span class="italic">CHAPTER VII</span></h2>
<p id="L_2016119EN.01000101-d-019" class="ti-section-2"><strong><span class="bold"><span class="italic">Cooperation and consistency</span></span></strong></p>
<h3 id="d1e5275-1-1" class="ti-section-1"><span class="expanded">Section 1</span></h3>
<p id="L_2016119EN.01000101-d-020" class="ti-section-2"><strong><span class="bold"><span class="expanded">Cooperation</span></span></strong></p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_60"></a>Article 60</h4>
<p class="sti-art">Cooperation between the lead supervisory authority and the other supervisory authorities concerned</p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The lead supervisory authority shall cooperate with the other supervisory authorities concerned in accordance with this Article in an endeavour to reach consensus. The lead supervisory authority and the supervisory authorities concerned shall exchange all relevant information with each other.</p>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The lead supervisory authority may request at any time other supervisory authorities concerned to provide mutual assistance pursuant to Article 61 and may conduct joint operations pursuant to Article 62, in particular for carrying out investigations or for monitoring the implementation of a measure concerning a controller or processor established in another Member State.</p>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The lead supervisory authority shall, without delay, communicate the relevant information on the matter to the other supervisory authorities concerned. It shall without delay submit a draft decision to the other supervisory authorities concerned for their opinion and take due account of their views.</p>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where any of the other supervisory authorities concerned within a period of four weeks after having been consulted in accordance with paragraph 3 of this Article, expresses a relevant and reasoned objection to the draft decision, the lead supervisory authority shall, if it does not follow the relevant and reasoned objection or is of the opinion that the objection is not relevant or reasoned, submit the matter to the consistency mechanism referred to in Article 63.</p>
<p class="normal">5.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where the lead supervisory authority intends to follow the relevant and reasoned objection made, it shall submit to the other supervisory authorities concerned a revised draft decision for their opinion. That revised draft decision shall be subject to the procedure referred to in paragraph&nbsp;4 within a period of two weeks.</p>
<p class="normal">6.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where none of the other supervisory authorities concerned has objected to the draft decision submitted by the lead supervisory authority within the period referred to in paragraphs&nbsp;4 and 5, the lead supervisory authority and the supervisory authorities concerned shall be deemed to be in agreement with that draft decision and shall be bound by it.</p>
<p class="normal">7.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The lead supervisory authority shall adopt and notify the decision to the main establishment or single establishment of the controller or processor, as the case may be and inform the other supervisory authorities concerned and the Board of the decision in question, including a summary of the relevant facts and grounds. The supervisory authority with which a complaint has been lodged shall inform the complainant on the decision.</p>
<p class="normal">8.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;By derogation from paragraph 7, where a complaint is dismissed or rejected, the supervisory authority with which the complaint was lodged shall adopt the decision and notify it to the complainant and shall inform the controller thereof.</p>
<p class="normal">9.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where the lead supervisory authority and the supervisory authorities concerned agree to dismiss or reject parts of a complaint and to act on other parts of that complaint, a separate decision shall be adopted for each of those parts of the matter. The lead supervisory authority shall adopt the decision for the part concerning actions in relation to the controller, shall notify it to the main establishment or single establishment of the controller or processor on the territory of its Member State and shall inform the complainant thereof, while the supervisory authority of the complainant shall adopt the decision for the part concerning dismissal or rejection of that complaint, and shall notify it to that complainant and shall inform the controller or processor thereof.</p>
<p class="normal">10.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;After being notified of the decision of the lead supervisory authority pursuant to paragraphs 7 and 9, the controller or processor shall take the necessary measures to ensure compliance with the decision as regards processing activities in the context of all its establishments in the Union. The controller or processor shall notify the measures taken for complying with the decision to the lead supervisory authority, which shall inform the other supervisory authorities concerned.</p>
<p class="normal">11.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where, in exceptional circumstances, a supervisory authority concerned has reasons to consider that there is an urgent need to act in order to protect the interests of data subjects, the urgency procedure referred to in Article 66 shall apply.</p>
<p class="normal">12.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The lead supervisory authority and the other supervisory authorities concerned shall supply the information required under this Article to each other by electronic means, using a standardised format.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_61"></a>Article 61</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Mutual assistance</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Supervisory authorities shall provide each other with relevant information and mutual assistance in order to implement and apply this Regulation in a consistent manner, and shall put in place measures for effective cooperation with one another. Mutual assistance shall cover, in particular, information requests and supervisory measures, such as requests to carry out prior authorisations and consultations, inspections and investigations.</p>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Each supervisory authority shall take all appropriate measures required to reply to a request of another supervisory authority without undue delay and no later than one month after receiving the request. Such measures may include, in particular, the transmission of relevant information on the conduct of an investigation.</p>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Requests for assistance shall contain all the necessary information, including the purpose of and reasons for the request. Information exchanged shall be used only for the purpose for which it was requested.</p>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The requested supervisory authority shall not refuse to comply with the request unless:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">it is not competent for the subject-matter of the request or for the measures it is requested to execute; or</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">compliance with the request would infringe this Regulation or Union or Member&nbsp;State law to which the supervisory authority receiving the request is subject.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">5.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The requested supervisory authority shall inform the requesting supervisory authority of the results or, as the case may be, of the progress of the measures taken in order to respond to the request. The requested supervisory authority shall provide reasons for any refusal to comply with a request pursuant to paragraph&nbsp;4.</p>
<p class="normal">6.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Requested supervisory authorities shall, as a rule, supply the information requested by other supervisory authorities by electronic means, using a standardised format.</p>
<p class="normal">7.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Requested supervisory authorities shall not charge a fee for any action taken by them pursuant to a request for mutual assistance. Supervisory authorities may agree on rules to indemnify each other for specific expenditure arising from the provision of mutual assistance in exceptional circumstances.</p>
<p class="normal">8.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where a supervisory authority does not provide the information referred to in paragraph&nbsp;5 of this Article within one month of receiving the request of another supervisory authority, the requesting supervisory authority may adopt a provisional measure on the territory of its Member State in accordance with Article&nbsp;55(1). In that case, the urgent need to act under Article&nbsp;66(1) shall be presumed to be met and require an urgent binding decision from the Board pursuant to Article&nbsp;66(2).</p>
<p class="normal">9.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Commission may, by means of implementing acts, specify the format and procedures for mutual assistance referred to in this Article and the arrangements for the exchange of information by electronic means between supervisory authorities, and between supervisory authorities and the Board, in particular the standardised format referred to in paragraph&nbsp;6 of this Article. Those implementing acts shall be adopted in accordance with the examination procedure referred to in Article&nbsp;93(2).</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_62"></a>Article 62</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Joint operations of supervisory authorities</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The supervisory authorities shall, where appropriate, conduct joint operations including joint investigations and joint enforcement measures in which members or staff of the supervisory authorities of other Member States are involved.</p>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where the controller or processor has establishments in several Member&nbsp;States or where a significant number of data subjects in more than one Member State are likely to be substantially affected by processing operations, a supervisory authority of each of those Member States shall have the right to participate in joint operations. The supervisory authority which is competent pursuant to Article&nbsp;56(1) or (4) shall invite the supervisory authority of each of those Member States to take part in the joint operations and shall respond without delay to the request of a supervisory authority to participate.</p>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;A supervisory authority may, in accordance with Member&nbsp;State law, and with the seconding supervisory authority’s authorisation, confer powers, including investigative powers on the seconding supervisory authority’s members or staff involved in joint operations or, in so far as the law of the Member&nbsp;State of the host supervisory authority permits, allow the seconding supervisory authority’s members or staff to exercise their investigative powers in accordance with the law of the Member&nbsp;State of the seconding supervisory authority. Such investigative powers may be exercised only under the guidance and in the presence of members or staff of the host supervisory authority. The seconding supervisory authority’s members or staff shall be subject to the Member&nbsp;State law of the host supervisory authority.</p>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where, in accordance with paragraph 1, staff of a seconding supervisory authority operate in another Member State, the Member&nbsp;State of the host supervisory authority shall assume responsibility for their actions, including liability, for any damage caused by them during their operations, in accordance with the law of the Member&nbsp;State in whose territory they are operating.</p>
<p class="normal">5.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Member State in whose territory the damage was caused shall make good such damage under the conditions applicable to damage caused by its own staff. The Member&nbsp;State of the seconding supervisory authority whose staff has caused damage to any person in the territory of another Member&nbsp;State shall reimburse that other Member&nbsp;State in full any sums it has paid to the persons entitled on their behalf.</p>
<p class="normal">6.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Without prejudice to the exercise of its rights&nbsp;<span class="italic">vis-à-vis</span>&nbsp;third parties and with the exception of paragraph&nbsp;5, each Member&nbsp;State shall refrain, in the case provided for in paragraph&nbsp;1, from requesting reimbursement from another Member&nbsp;State in relation to damage referred to in paragraph 4.</p>
<p class="normal">7.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where a joint operation is intended and a supervisory authority does not, within one month, comply with the obligation laid down in the second sentence of paragraph&nbsp;2 of this Article, the other supervisory authorities may adopt a provisional measure on the territory of its Member State in accordance with Article 55. In that case, the urgent need to act under Article 66(1) shall be presumed to be met and require an opinion or an urgent binding decision from the Board pursuant to Article 66(2).</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h3 id="d1e5459-1-1" class="ti-section-1"><span class="expanded">Section 2</span></h3>
<p id="L_2016119EN.01000101-d-021" class="ti-section-2"><strong><span class="bold"><span class="expanded">Consistency</span></span></strong></p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_63"></a>Article 63</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Consistency mechanism</strong></p>
<p class="normal">In order to contribute to the consistent application of this Regulation throughout the Union, the supervisory authorities shall cooperate with each other and, where relevant, with the Commission, through the consistency mechanism as set out in this Section.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_64"></a>Article 64</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Opinion of the Board</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Board shall issue an opinion where a competent supervisory authority intends to adopt any of the measures below. To that end, the competent supervisory authority shall communicate the draft decision to the Board, when it:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">aims to adopt a list of the processing operations subject to the requirement for a data protection impact assessment pursuant to Article 35(4);</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">concerns a matter pursuant to Article&nbsp;40(7) whether a draft code of conduct or an amendment or extension to a code of conduct complies with this Regulation;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">aims to approve the criteria for accreditation of a body pursuant to Article&nbsp;41(3) or a certification body pursuant to Article&nbsp;43(3);</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(d)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">aims to determine standard data protection clauses referred to in point&nbsp;(d) of Article&nbsp;46(2) and in Article 28(8);</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(e)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">aims to authorise contractual clauses referred to in point (a) of Article&nbsp;46(3); or</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(f)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">aims to approve binding corporate rules within the meaning of Article&nbsp;47.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Any supervisory authority, the Chair of the Board or the Commission may request that any matter of general application or producing effects in more than one Member&nbsp;State be examined by the Board with a view to obtaining an opinion, in particular where a competent supervisory authority does not comply with the obligations for mutual assistance in accordance with Article&nbsp;61 or for joint operations in accordance with Article&nbsp;62.</p>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In the cases referred to in paragraphs 1 and 2, the Board shall issue an opinion on the matter submitted to it provided that it has not already issued an opinion on the same matter. That opinion shall be adopted within eight weeks by simple majority of the members of the Board. That period may be extended by a further six weeks, taking into account the complexity of the subject matter. Regarding the draft decision referred to in paragraph&nbsp;1 circulated to the members of the Board in accordance with paragraph&nbsp;5, a member which has not objected within a reasonable period indicated by the Chair, shall be deemed to be in agreement with the draft decision.</p>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Supervisory authorities and the Commission shall, without undue delay, communicate by electronic means to the Board, using a standardised format any relevant information, including as the case may be a summary of the facts, the draft decision, the grounds which make the enactment of such measure necessary, and the views of other supervisory authorities concerned.</p>
<p class="normal">5.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Chair of the Board shall, without undue, delay inform by electronic means:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the members of the Board and the Commission of any relevant information which has been communicated to it using a standardised format. The secretariat of the Board shall, where necessary, provide translations of relevant information; and</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">the supervisory authority referred to, as the case may be, in paragraphs&nbsp;1 and 2, and the Commission of the opinion and make it public.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">6.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The competent supervisory authority shall not adopt its draft decision referred to in paragraph 1 within the period referred to in paragraph 3.</p>
<p class="normal">7.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The supervisory authority referred to in paragraph 1 shall take utmost account of the opinion of the Board and shall, within two weeks after receiving the opinion, communicate to the Chair of the Board by electronic means whether it will maintain or amend its draft decision and, if any, the amended draft decision, using a standardised format.</p>
<p class="normal">8.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where the supervisory authority concerned informs the Chair of the Board within the period referred to in paragraph 7 of this Article that it does not intend to follow the opinion of the Board, in whole or in part, providing the relevant grounds, Article&nbsp;65(1) shall apply.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_65"></a>Article 65</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Dispute resolution by the Board</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In order to ensure the correct and consistent application of this Regulation in individual cases, the Board shall adopt a binding decision in the following cases:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">where, in a case referred to in Article 60(4), a supervisory authority concerned has raised a relevant and reasoned objection to a draft decision of the lead authority or the lead authority has rejected such an objection as being not relevant or reasoned. The binding decision shall concern all the matters which are the subject of the relevant and reasoned objection, in particular whether there is an infringement of this Regulation;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">where there are conflicting views on which of the supervisory authorities concerned is competent for the main establishment;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">where a competent supervisory authority does not request the opinion of the Board in the cases referred to in Article&nbsp;64(1), or does not follow the opinion of the Board issued under Article&nbsp;64. In that case, any supervisory authority concerned or the Commission may communicate the matter to the Board.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The decision referred to in paragraph 1 shall be adopted within one month from the referral of the subject-matter by a two-thirds majority of the members of the Board. That period may be extended by a further month on account of the complexity of the subject-matter. The decision referred to in paragraph 1 shall be reasoned and addressed to the lead supervisory authority and all the supervisory authorities concerned and binding on them.</p>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where the Board has been unable to adopt a decision within the periods referred to in paragraph&nbsp;2, it shall adopt its decision within two weeks following the expiration of the second month referred to in paragraph 2 by a simple majority of the members of the Board. Where the members of the Board are split, the decision shall by adopted by the vote of its Chair.</p>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The supervisory authorities concerned shall not adopt a decision on the subject matter submitted to the Board under paragraph 1 during the periods referred to in paragraphs&nbsp;2 and&nbsp;3.</p>
<p class="normal">5.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Chair of the Board shall notify, without undue delay, the decision referred to in paragraph 1 to the supervisory authorities concerned. It shall inform the Commission thereof. The decision shall be published on the website of the Board without delay after the supervisory authority has notified the final decision referred to in paragraph&nbsp;6.</p>
<p class="normal">6.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The lead supervisory authority or, as the case may be, the supervisory authority with which the complaint has been lodged shall adopt its final decision on the basis of the decision referred to in paragraph 1 of this Article, without undue delay and at the latest by one month after the Board has notified its decision. The lead supervisory authority or, as the case may be, the supervisory authority with which the complaint has been lodged, shall inform the Board of the date when its final decision is notified respectively to the controller or the processor and to the data subject. The final decision of the supervisory authorities concerned shall be adopted under the terms of Article&nbsp;60(7), (8) and&nbsp;(9). The final decision shall refer to the decision referred to in paragraph&nbsp;1 of this Article and shall specify that the decision referred to in that paragraph will be published on the website of the Board in accordance with paragraph 5 of this Article. The final decision shall attach the decision referred to in paragraph&nbsp;1 of this Article.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_66"></a>Article 66</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Urgency procedure</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In exceptional circumstances, where a supervisory authority concerned considers that there is an urgent need to act in order to protect the rights and freedoms of data subjects, it may, by way of derogation from the consistency mechanism referred to in Articles&nbsp;63, 64 and 65 or the procedure referred to in Article&nbsp;60, immediately adopt provisional measures intended to produce legal effects on its own territory with a specified period of validity which shall not exceed three months. The supervisory authority shall, without delay, communicate those measures and the reasons for adopting them to the other supervisory authorities concerned, to the Board and to the Commission.</p>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where a supervisory authority has taken a measure pursuant to paragraph&nbsp;1 and considers that final measures need urgently be adopted, it may request an urgent opinion or an urgent binding decision from the Board, giving reasons for requesting such opinion or decision.</p>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Any supervisory authority may request an urgent opinion or an urgent binding decision, as the case may be, from the Board where a competent supervisory authority has not taken an appropriate measure in a situation where there is an urgent need to act, in order to protect the rights and freedoms of data subjects, giving reasons for requesting such opinion or decision, including for the urgent need to act.</p>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;By derogation from Article&nbsp;64(3) and Article 65(2), an urgent opinion or an urgent binding decision referred to in paragraphs&nbsp;2 and&nbsp;3 of this Article shall be adopted within two weeks by simple majority of the members of the Board.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_67"></a>Article 67</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Exchange of information</strong></p>
<p class="normal">The Commission may adopt implementing acts of general scope in order to specify the arrangements for the exchange of information by electronic means between supervisory authorities, and between supervisory authorities and the Board, in particular the standardised format referred to in Article&nbsp;64.</p>
<p class="normal">Those implementing acts shall be adopted in accordance with the examination procedure referred to in Article&nbsp;93(2).</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<h3 id="d1e5663-1-1" class="ti-section-1"><span class="expanded">Section 3</span></h3>
<p id="L_2016119EN.01000101-d-022" class="ti-section-2"><strong><span class="bold"><span class="expanded">European data protection board</span></span></strong></p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_68"></a>Article 68</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>European Data Protection Board</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The European Data Protection Board (the ‘Board’) is hereby established as a body of the Union and shall have legal personality.</p>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Board shall be represented by its Chair.</p>
<p class="normal">3.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Board shall be composed of the head of one supervisory authority of each Member&nbsp;State and of the European Data Protection Supervisor, or their respective representatives.</p>
<p class="normal">4.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Where in a Member State more than one supervisory authority is responsible for monitoring the application of the provisions pursuant to this Regulation, a joint representative shall be appointed in accordance with that Member State’s law.</p>
<p class="normal">5.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Commission shall have the right to participate in the activities and meetings of the Board without voting right. The Commission shall designate a representative. The Chair of the Board shall communicate to the Commission the activities of the Board.</p>
<p class="normal">6.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;In the cases referred to in Article 65, the European Data Protection Supervisor shall have voting rights only on decisions which concern principles and rules applicable to the Union institutions, bodies, offices and agencies which correspond in substance to those of this Regulation.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_69"></a>Article 69</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Independence</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Board shall act independently when performing its tasks or exercising its powers pursuant to Articles 70 and&nbsp;71.</p>
<p class="normal">2.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Without prejudice to requests by the Commission referred to in point (b) of Article 70(1) and in Article 70(2), the Board shall, in the performance of its tasks or the exercise of its powers, neither seek nor take instructions from anybody.</p>
<h4 id="d1e1384-1-1" class="ti-art"><a name="article_70"></a>Article 70</h4>
<p class="sti-art"><strong>Tasks of the Board</strong></p>
<p class="normal">1.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Board shall ensure the consistent application of this Regulation. To that end, the Board shall, on its own initiative or, where relevant, at the request of the Commission, in particular:</p>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(a)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">monitor and ensure the correct application of this Regulation in the cases provided for in Articles 64 and 65 without prejudice to the tasks of national supervisory authorities;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(b)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">advise the Commission on any issue related to the protection of personal data in the Union, including on any proposed amendment of this Regulation;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(c)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">advise the Commission on the format and procedures for the exchange of information between controllers, processors and supervisory authorities for binding corporate rules;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(d)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">issue guidelines, recommendations, and best practices on procedures for erasing links, copies or replications of personal data from publicly available communication services as referred to in Article 17(2);</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(e)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">examine, on its own initiative, on request of one of its members or on request of the Commission, any question covering the application of this Regulation and issue guidelines, recommendations and best practices in order to encourage consistent application of this Regulation;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(f)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">issue guidelines, recommendations and best practices in accordance with point&nbsp;(e) of this paragraph for further specifying the criteria and conditions for decisions based on profiling pursuant to Article 22(2);</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(g)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">issue guidelines, recommendations and best practices in accordance with point&nbsp;(e) of this paragraph for establishing the personal data breaches and determining the undue delay referred to in Article 33(1) and (2) and for the particular circumstances in which a controller or a processor is required to notify the personal data breach;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(h)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">issue guidelines, recommendations and best practices in accordance with point&nbsp;(e) of this paragraph as to the circumstances in which a personal data breach is likely to result in a high risk to the rights and freedoms of the natural persons referred to in Article 34(1).</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(i)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">issue guidelines, recommendations and best practices in accordance with point&nbsp;(e) of this paragraph for the purpose of further specifying the criteria and requirements for personal data transfers based on binding corporate rules adhered to by controllers and binding corporate rules adhered to by processors and on further necessary requirements to ensure the protection of personal data of the data subjects concerned referred to in Article 47;</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">

<col width="4%">

</td>

<p class="normal">issue guidelines, recommendations and best practices in accordance with point&nbsp;(e) of this paragraph for the purpose of further specifying the criteria and requirements for the personal data transfers on the basis of Article 49(1);</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(k)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">draw up guidelines for supervisory authorities concerning the application of measures referred to in Article 58(1), (2) and (3) and the setting of administrative fines pursuant to Article 83;</p>
</td>

<colgroup>
<col width="4%">
<col width="96%"></colgroup>
<tbody>

</td>

<p class="normal">review the practical application of the guidelines, recommendations and best practices referred to in points (e) and&nbsp;(f);</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<table border="0" width="100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<colgroup>
<col width="4%">

<tr>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">(m)</p>
</td>
<td valign="top">
<p class="normal">issue guidelines, recommendations and best practices in accordance with point&nbsp;(e) of this paragraph for establishing common procedures for reporting by natural persons of infringements of this Regulation pursuant to Article 54(2);</p>
</td>
</tr>

</td>

</td>
</tr>

</td>
